Some<span class='line-break'> </span> of their children has very<span class='line-break'> </span> bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to meet his daughter at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.  He went on the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>

<div id="page-1163">
<h3><a name="page-1163">Monday February  7, 1921</a></h3>

She<span class='line-break'> </span> did not stay long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-1164">
<h3><a name="page-1164">Tuesday February  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on their <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> load on some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8056' title='Mr Cothram'>Mr Cothram</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> look at a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.  He did not<span class='line-break'> </span> decide what he would do about<span class='line-break'> </span> takeing her.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed all<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  Some thing that<span class='line-break'> </span> she should not do if I could <span class='line-break'> </span> help it but I cant.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was all of the family that<span class='line-break'> </span> I saw.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> was <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  Heard today that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutchersons</a> little pet <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.  I know they were<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry a bout it getting <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>killed</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1165">
<h3><a name="page-1165">Wednesday February  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rained</a> morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> hung up<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> ready to <a href='../subjects/8057' title='smoking'>smoke</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> hang up his.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then they <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the rest of the day.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Killed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and cooked <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is proud of it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Sam Owen</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with his last<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  I was uneasy<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout the tobacco.  So a <span class='line-break'> </span> fraid it would get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> It <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> very well and<span class='line-break'> </span> he got home about night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and Edna went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1166">
<h3><a name="page-1166">Thursday February 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  Rained about<span class='line-break'> </span> all day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a> now.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  Finished a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>Mended</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> One of the <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> got hurt<span class='line-break'> </span> some way this evening.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> it will get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-1167">
<h3><a name="page-1167">Friday February 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  Finished one of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a> cureings.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8058' title='Wesley Cothran'>Mr Wesley Cothran</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> and got a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> today, the<span class='line-break'> </span> cow that I bought from <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some today<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some tonight.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-1168">
<h3><a name="page-1168">Saturday February 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut</a> and <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the cut paper tree up for<span class='line-break'> </span> wood.  It was a job that<span class='line-break'> </span> kept them busy all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and set by the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this evening.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> got some <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8060' title='Miss Roles'>Miss Roles</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two of them was for Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope he may have<span class='line-break'> </span> good luck with them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1169">
<h3><a name="page-1169">Sunday February 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> for the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and got two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.  They packed down<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields and spent the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar</a> come after me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come up there<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I was so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come as I<span class='line-break'> </span> could come home and not<span class='line-break'> </span> be any trouble to any one.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> had a good <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula</a> and <a href='../subjects/8061' title='Leslie William Roark'>her husband</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  They are lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  I hope that they will <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin &amp; family went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>John Smiths</a>.  Hope they had<span class='line-break'> </span> a pleasant day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1170">
<h3><a name="page-1170">Monday February 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed a hog</a> for Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Sam Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from here today.  I felt<span class='line-break'> </span> sad to see them go but<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he has bettered<span class='line-break'> </span> him self.  He moved to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8062' title='George Allen'>Mr George Allens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I fixed up after<span class='line-break'> </span> hog killing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She carrie[d]<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> was there<span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  I would of<span class='line-break'> </span> like to see them all.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would be glad to see all<span class='line-break'> </span> of the children.  I may never <span class='line-break'> </span> see them all any more.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1171">
<h3><a name="page-1171">Tuesday February 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> burnt a <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a>.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> finished the bed.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> to <a href='../subjects/7541' title='Mt. Airy, Virginia'>Mt Airy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for me and then started<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Was going to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to Danville today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8063' title='John Tucker'>John Tucker</a> carried some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> for Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> carried his <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a><span class='line-break'> </span> from here today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> ground<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7622' title='sausage'>sausage</a> and seasoned it.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today I made <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scrapple</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I sent 4 roosters and 4<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> to the store.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have a <a href='../subjects/276' title='rooster'>rooster</a> that <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>John<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> raised.  I am to pay<span class='line-break'> </span> three dollars for him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1172">
<h3><a name="page-1172">Wednesday February 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> was in <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Solde some <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a>.  Missed the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7991' title='train'>train</a> that he aimed to come on<span class='line-break'> </span> but got to come on a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We was all very glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> he got home.  He was not pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> with the sales of his tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> of clothes today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola<span class='line-break'> </span> Jefferson</a>.  I was glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> hear from her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim has gone to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to help him burn a plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1173">
<h3><a name="page-1173">Thursday February 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked corn</a> all day or a bout.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went and shucked one shock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> both had a hand getting<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Josie baked a <a href='../subjects/46' title='pudding'>cream puding</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was fine.  This evening I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  She did not stay<span class='line-break'> </span> late.  I was glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Osker</a> come down here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar</a> brough Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>clover seed</a>.  He got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  They had company <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1174">
<h3><a name="page-1174">Friday February 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> [and] <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7736' title='hauling feed'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> feed</a> and a load of <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening to meet<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  We carried<span class='line-break'> </span> 12 <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> and 7 doz <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We bought several things.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that Nell<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Evylin come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> Would like to see them<span class='line-break'> </span> all but cant tell when<span class='line-break'> </span> that will be.  May not <span class='line-break'> </span> ever see them a gain<span class='line-break'> </span> but hope I will.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1175">
<h3><a name="page-1175">Saturday February 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad evening.  <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>Hail</a> and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/8064' title='cutting stalks'>cut stalks</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I boiled<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> at the <a href='../subjects/7624' title='wash house'>wash<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> and burnt some bre[ad?].<span class='line-break'> </span> Evlyn made some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> poped some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> is foolish a bout <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She is good to <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Ben &amp; Jim put some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> after it<span class='line-break'> </span> commenced to rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1176">
<h3><a name="page-1176">Sunday February 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>Hail</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> and <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snow</a>.  The trees was<span class='line-break'> </span> covered with <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a>.  Cleaned up<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until evening then<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They was going home on the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7991' title='train'>train</a>.  Ben &amp; Josie got home<span class='line-break'> </span> some time be fore night.<span class='line-break'> </span> We enjoyed Nell &amp; Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> stay with us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> a good one.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> for me today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1177">
<h3><a name="page-1177">Monday February 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  Colde and<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snow</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Josie and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> ordered<span class='line-break'> </span> them a <a href='../subjects/8029' title='phonograph'>musick box</a> a peice.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> hope that they may get them<span class='line-break'> </span> ok.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I boiled<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7613' title='hogs head'>hogs face</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/167' title='hogs feet'>feet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have tacked a few <a href='../subjects/196' title='rags'>rags</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/197' title='rugs'>rug</a> if I ever get it made.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today is 56 years a go I was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1178">
<h3><a name="page-1178">Tuesday February 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>Snow</a> a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> all gone.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on her <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I made two<span class='line-break'> </span> bolster slips and seven<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/127' title='pillow'>pillow</a> slips.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1179">
<h3><a name="page-1179">Wednesday February 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and a little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They put all<span class='line-break'> </span> the tobacco in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> is to strip.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1180">
<h3><a name="page-1180">Thursday February 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> colde day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> had a good dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  While she <span class='line-break'> </span> was here <a href='../subjects/8065' title='Dave Walker'>Dave Walker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come.  He had not bin here<span class='line-break'> </span> in several years.  We was<span class='line-break'> </span> all glad to see him but<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry that they had put<span class='line-break'> </span> him off his job.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> is here tonight.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> are all in the dineing<span class='line-break'> </span> room talking.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry has gone to Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> to night to stay a while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floid Reynols</a> and <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> is there to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1181">
<h3><a name="page-1181">Friday February 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> colde day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8065' title='Dave Walker'>Dave Walker</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried them to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come and all of <span class='line-break'> </span> the children a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a> come in<span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so anxious to see<span class='line-break'> </span> all of the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> It keeps so colde that I<span class='line-break'> </span> cant go to see them and<span class='line-break'> </span> they dont come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben got <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>wood</a> and <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/7624' title='wash house'>wash house</a> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1182">
<h3><a name="page-1182">Saturday February 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde and partly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> and hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped some.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went to <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mount Airy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He rode <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children come.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Carrie made some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  They made peanut<span class='line-break'> </span> and walnut candy.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> was very nice and good.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/352' title='Jim Doss'>Mr Doss</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>was killed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Blown up by a lighting<span class='line-break'> </span> tank at <a href='../subjects/8066' title='Mr Irby'>Mr Irbys</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1183">
<h3><a name="page-1183">Sunday February 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> packed<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> down ready to<span class='line-break'> </span> load on the <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a>.  <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>Shucked<span class='line-break'> </span> some corn</a>.  Helped a man get<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> out of the mud.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hitched <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> to the car and pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> it out.  Went to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I went to Marvin.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>, <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>, and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> went.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that a childe<span class='line-break'> </span> was burnt to <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>death</a> at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8067' title='Clyde Reynolds'>Clide Reynols's</a>.  No one know<span class='line-break'> </span> what will happen in a day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel glad when all is<span class='line-break'> </span> reasonable well and have<span class='line-break'> </span> enough of things to be<span class='line-break'> </span> comfortable.  I wish I <span class='line-break'> </span> could be more thankful and<span class='line-break'> </span> more humble than I am.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> comed my hair today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1184">
<h3><a name="page-1184">Monday February 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a> to day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> loaded on his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> on <a href='../subjects/8063' title='John Tucker'>John<span class='line-break'> </span> Tuckers</a> <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> intends going to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salet</a>.  The first <span class='line-break'> </span> that we have had this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  While I<span class='line-break'> </span> was there a man came and <span class='line-break'> </span> bought a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> from him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack Hubbard</a> moved to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> today.  I hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> may do well and it will<span class='line-break'> </span> be for <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kates</a> good two.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so anxious to<span class='line-break'> </span> know how every one is<span class='line-break'> </span> getting on.  It keeps so<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> that I cant get<span class='line-break'> </span> out much yet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />

<div id="page-1186">
<h3><a name="page-1186">Tuesday March  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> carried his <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> to <a href='../subjects/7661' title='Gilmore Scruggs'>Mr Scrugs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and solde him the <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> had started to ship the calf.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim carried a box of <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> send to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> for his folks.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'> solde the last of his<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> in Danvill to day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They bought several things.<span class='line-break'> </span> Got home at dark.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they are all at<span class='line-break'> </span> home and all are well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid here with <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> until twelve<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock.  <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come in a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I do want<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> so<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  I will go over as soon as I can.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1187">
<h3><a name="page-1187">Wednesday March  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked corn</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Cut <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and eat dinner then<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate and I went to see <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mag and the two little <span class='line-break'> </span> children was at home.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> other children was at school.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbard</a> covered a shed to one<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>houses</a> today.  I come<span class='line-break'> </span> by to see <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; Kate a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <a href='../subjects/435' title='James Farthing'>Jim Fargthing</a>[?] had<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/261' title='cutting match'>cutting match</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I rode on a <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> with a<span class='line-break'> </span> stranger as far as <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie are putting<span class='line-break'> </span> up a <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>stove</a> that they bought<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1188">
<h3><a name="page-1188">Thursday March  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A changable day.  Clear tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> and the <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> blowing.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7721' title='hauling stalks'>hauled stalks</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Ben <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled wood</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Jim <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> in the <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>oil<span class='line-break'> </span> stove</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found her sitting up.  She looks<span class='line-break'> </span> feeble.  She is <a href='../subjects/164' title='improving'>improving</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> They have a col woman staying <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  They were making a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canvas</a> for the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant beds</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> stopd here a<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  We all are all<span class='line-break'> </span> ways glad to see her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1189">
<h3><a name="page-1189">Friday March  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big<span class='line-break'> </span> washing for her to have to do.  She should<span class='line-break'> </span> not wash if I could help it.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> washed yesterday and a gain this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I do wish they could<span class='line-break'> </span> get some one to do that much<span class='line-break'> </span> for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8071' title='Mrs Kent'>Mrs Kent</a> come this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> came by and<span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Kent went with her<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She said Carrie was bakeing<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben &amp; Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin has gone to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to a <a href='../subjects/8072' title='Farmers Union'>farmers<span class='line-break'> </span> union</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1190">
<h3><a name="page-1190">Saturday March  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day with two <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> plowed some in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and plowed for a <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a><span class='line-break'> </span> patch.  Tonight Jim &amp; Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> dressed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She bathed the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> and <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I was glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> see the children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strait Stone.  The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8074' title='Mr Lee'>Mr Lee</a> is there tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1191">
<h3><a name="page-1191">Sunday March  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> blowed<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  We all staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> come.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  We was glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Lizzie and Earl has just<span class='line-break'> </span> started home.  Ten oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone this morning to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8074' title='Mr Lee'>Mr Lee</a><span class='line-break'> </span> preached his farewell<span class='line-break'> </span> sermond at that place.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1192">
<h3><a name="page-1192">Monday March  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/8075' title='sowing grass'>sowed</a> grass<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> things in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> &amp; a <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a> patch.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  This evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> was not<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  I had a pleasant time<span class='line-break'> </span> with the girls.  I stoped at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutchersons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/244' title='Mrs Mayhew'>Mrs Mayhew</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  I am glad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> is able to get round that much.<span class='line-break'> </span> I enjoyed being with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and her and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come here.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry that I was not<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  Marvin went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the<span class='line-break'> </span> Iland</a> for a <a href='../subjects/8029' title='phonograph'>phonogapt</a> for Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Josie.  Ben and Josie have<span class='line-break'> </span> gone up there to night and I <span class='line-break'> </span> dont know when they are coming<span class='line-break'> </span> back.  <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> stayed a wake until<span class='line-break'> </span> after nine oclock.  Marvin solde <a href='../subjects/8076' title='Jerrie'>Jerrie</a> [Jennie?]<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1193">
<h3><a name="page-1193">Tuesday March  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a>.  Made<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a> some under bodies.<span class='line-break'> </span> I potered a round until<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Then I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> drove<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  We had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> trip.  Bought a few<span class='line-break'> </span> things.  <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> in a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7241' title='Eula Mayhew'>Eula Mayhew</a> come in a<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7923' title='hauling corn'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a load of <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Ben has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> playing the <a href='../subjects/8029' title='phonograph'>musick box</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  I enjoy hearing<span class='line-break'> </span> it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1194">
<h3><a name="page-1194">Wednesday March  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  The first thunder<span class='line-break'> </span> cloud of the year.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> did not go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled</a> some <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> bought <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/8078' title='heifer'>heifer</a> from <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Jim &amp; Ben <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening until it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; Carrie went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip patch</a> to cut <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It rained and they had<span class='line-break'> </span> to quit.  I went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canvas</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> the plant bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1195">
<h3><a name="page-1195">Thursday March 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> put the <a href='../subjects/418' title='canvas'>canvas</a> on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant beds</a> to day.  They <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> some trees</a> at the <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for wood.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She baked some nice <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and the children and<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was washing. <span class='line-break'> </span> She quit.  Will finish in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning if nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> happens.  She come with<span class='line-break'> </span> us to the <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip patch</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and cut <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8079' title='suit'>suit</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a big <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1196">
<h3><a name="page-1196">Friday March 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  She got done<span class='line-break'> </span> by 11 oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the little children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> come a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Heard to day that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posise</a> got hurt.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that he may get on<span class='line-break'> </span> better than is expected.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry for him<span class='line-break'> </span> and his folks.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>Frost</a> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1197">
<h3><a name="page-1197">Saturday March 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and part of the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I borrowed<span class='line-break'> </span> a bucket of <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8080' title='C. R. Warren'>Mr C R Waren</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>to speak</a> there tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Warren &amp; Berger come<span class='line-break'> </span> but no crowd to speak to.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1198">
<h3><a name="page-1198">Sunday March 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  We all<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home until noon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had company both olde<span class='line-break'> </span> and young.  <a href='../subjects/7459' title='Asa Anderson'>Acie</a> and <a href='../subjects/8082' title='Hessie Anderson'>Hessie<span class='line-break'> </span> Anderson</a>, <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a>, <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a>, and <a href='../subjects/8043' title='Virginia Moses'>Miss Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Moses</a>; Ben and his crowd<span class='line-break'> </span> and I; <a href='../subjects/933' title='Walter Carr'>Mr Walter Car</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8083' title='Jo Hobson'>Mr Jo Hobson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> folks today.  I miss<span class='line-break'> </span> them most (much) as I would my<span class='line-break'> </span> folks at home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1199">
<h3><a name="page-1199">Monday March 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked<span class='line-break'> </span> corn</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she washed<span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/8032' title='dining room'>dineing room</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> floor.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> called me <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and said she<span class='line-break'> </span> could get a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> to take<span class='line-break'> </span> me <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  I was a fraid to<span class='line-break'> </span> go.  A fraid it would rain<span class='line-break'> </span> and it did.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that we did not go.  Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that some day I can go<span class='line-break'> </span> but so many things happen.<span class='line-break'> </span> I may never go a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7241' title='Eula Mayhew'>Eula Mayhew</a> is home tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to stay with <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> got his <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> mud so that Jim &amp; Ben had<span class='line-break'> </span> to help him get it out.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1200">
<h3><a name="page-1200">Tuesday March 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> about all day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then he went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  He carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> with him.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for herself to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> carried me.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> had a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> and <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a while.  Did <span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing worth<span class='line-break'> </span> anything.  We had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time any way.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has commenced to sleep <span class='line-break'> </span> up stairs.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1201">
<h3><a name="page-1201">Wednesday March 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished shucking <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin so troubled all day<span class='line-break'> </span> that she could not work<span class='line-break'> </span> much.  Poor little <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> last night though<span class='line-break'> </span> he would go to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a><span class='line-break'> </span> but he did not get off.<span class='line-break'> </span> His father brought him<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  We were all so glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to have him home again.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope he wont try it<span class='line-break'> </span> a gain soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> let her go<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> with her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1202">
<h3><a name="page-1202">Thursday March 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7736' title='hauling feed'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> feed</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  I got a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I finished<span class='line-break'> </span> getting out <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> and am glad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> as busy as she could be.<span class='line-break'> </span> The teacher <a href='../subjects/8084' title='Gordon McConnel'>Gordon McConnel</a> [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> is there to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had made all<span class='line-break'> </span> preperations for him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The first time that Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> ever went to school.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7964' title='Miss Carter'>Miss Carter</a> carried him &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> brought him home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I want to see all of<span class='line-break'> </span> the children so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> Doubt ever seeing them<span class='line-break'> </span> all a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1203">
<h3><a name="page-1203">Friday March 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> up their <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> by twelve oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> then Jim <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> and Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Bought a few things.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> stayed with <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  I was glad to<span class='line-break'> </span> see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Jim &amp; Ben &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> to a <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>meeting of<span class='line-break'> </span> the farmers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8094' title='Mr McCormic'>Mr McCormic</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at Marvins last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1204">
<h3><a name="page-1204">Saturday March 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
