<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> but no<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cleaned<span class='line-break'> </span> up land and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Mr Jim Emerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7672' title='Sarah Emerson'>Sarah Emerson</a> come today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> come this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> brought a basket of <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were glad to get them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> would of<span class='line-break'> </span> gone with me <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> if I could of went. <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> brought me two<span class='line-break'> </span> boxes from <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1205">
<h3><a name="page-1205">Sunday March 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  All of us staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until twelve oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr<span class='line-break'> </span> Wigginton</a> and <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> walked a round most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the evening.  <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> sent for the <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>dr</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wigginton</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Ben brought five<span class='line-break'> </span> nice <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> home with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to get them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/286' title='Mrs. Oley Hubbard'>Mrs Hubbard</a> tonight and<span class='line-break'> </span> will stay until Wednesday if<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing happens.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1206">
<h3><a name="page-1206">Monday March 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> March.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8095' title='Willie Allen'>Mr Willie Allen</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked corn</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have bin busy nearly <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is at <a href='../subjects/8096' title='Mr Hubbards'>Mr Hubbards</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I miss her and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> so much.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She had bin<span class='line-break'> </span> sweeping.  <a href='../subjects/8097' title='Harold Mayhew'>Harold Mayhew</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1207">
<h3><a name="page-1207">Tuesday March 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  Not so but<span class='line-break'> </span> what any one could work until<span class='line-break'> </span> late.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> cleaned up the land<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shucking his corn</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> put it in the <a href='../subjects/285' title='corn house'>corn house</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> What belonged to us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed some and got <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> to eat.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> come and<span class='line-break'> </span> got a setting of <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I get so lonesome when<span class='line-break'> </span> the most of the folks is<span class='line-break'> </span> gone that I dont know<span class='line-break'> </span> what to.  Hope <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> can<span class='line-break'> </span> com home to morrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1208">
<h3><a name="page-1208">Wednesday March 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/8098' title='harrowing'>harrowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> he went to <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a>.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  They got home<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout night.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on the ditch ba[?] getting<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> for winter.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  It is <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope it wont frost.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry has my paper.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1209">
<h3><a name="page-1209">Thursday March 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/8099' title='Mrs Reynolds'>Mrs Reynols</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to the burial with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She baked a <a href='../subjects/7723' title='molasses'>molasses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/46' title='pudding'>pudding</a>.  It was fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georg Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> and her <span class='line-break'> </span> children was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was makeing<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7727' title='Edith Ardena Craddock'>Edieth</a> a <a href='../subjects/7517' title='doll'>doll</a>.  Denia was<span class='line-break'> </span> bakeing light rolls.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8100' title='Willie Hutcherson'>Willie Hutcherson</a> and <a href='../subjects/8088' title='Lucy Hutcherson'>his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother</a> went to Mrs. Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> burial.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1210">
<h3><a name="page-1210">Friday March 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> stayed.  Ben got home a <span class='line-break'> </span> while before night.  Made the<span class='line-break'> </span> trip ok.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>, <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> and <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a pleasant evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> come after us with<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> in the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Caught five minowes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> washed the dishes.  <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> sent <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Ednas</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dresses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> home to day.  They are<span class='line-break'> </span> very nice.  Jims <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> layed to day for the first<span class='line-break'> </span> time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1211">
<h3><a name="page-1211">Saturday March 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> build a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> helped two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7562' title='Stuart Owen'>Stewart Owen</a> staid with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> awhile to day.  Eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed up her floor<span class='line-break'> </span> today and got the dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie</a> &amp; the babies.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She was<span class='line-break'> </span> washing.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> was helping<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is working on<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for <a href='../subjects/8101' title='Easter'>Easter</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1212">
<h3><a name="page-1212">Sunday March 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home.  <a href='../subjects/8102' title='Leslie Roark'>Leslie Roark</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladice</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> and <a href='../subjects/8103' title='Hildna'>Hildna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/8104' title='Emmet Brumfield'>Emmet Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> load to Gladice<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I am so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> he did it.  Gave some of them<span class='line-break'> </span> pleasure I know.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a> come for<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert</a> was driveing<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  I spent a <span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant day.  <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> had a nice <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to be thankful for all<span class='line-break'> </span> that is done for me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1213">
<h3><a name="page-1213">Monday March 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> and getting <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  He put wire a round<span class='line-break'> </span> the porch to keep <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> crawling through.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had an egg hunt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has done what cooking<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin done.  All of us<span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was there<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There has bin lots of <span class='line-break'> </span> passing here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7800' title='Roanoke, Virginia'>Roanoke</a> this evening.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> she may get well yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> We looked for <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> home.  He has not come<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1214">
<h3><a name="page-1214">Tuesday March 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> this morning.  I am expecting<span class='line-break'> </span> the fruit to be killed tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has not come yet.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> dont know what to think is the<span class='line-break'> </span> matter.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cleaned up the land<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.  They are in this<span class='line-break'> </span> room a sleep to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> a border on <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  She worked on a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had<span class='line-break'> </span> finished a dress for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1215">
<h3><a name="page-1215">Wednesday March 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> evening and rain<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  We had a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I am sorry but<span class='line-break'> </span> that was something that powerful<span class='line-break'> </span> man could not help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the island</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I got the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  We were very glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that he did.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was no one at <span class='line-break'> </span> home but <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> when<span class='line-break'> </span> I got there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went by <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was makeing <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> sent<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie some <a href='../subjects/8105' title='yeast'>yeast</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to make her some light<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1216">
<h3><a name="page-1216">Thursday March 31, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>light rolls</a>.  They were<span class='line-break'> </span> fine.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> worked <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazels</a> and Evas <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dresses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set a hen</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote two letters</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1217">
<h3><a name="page-1217">Friday April  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood</a> for flue wood.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  She made light<span class='line-break'> </span> rolls for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were very nice.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floid Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> coat.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I gess I have burnt<span class='line-break'> </span> over a hundred papers<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> put them<span class='line-break'> </span> a way for <a href='../subjects/213' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (1833-1904)'>her father</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I though some one would<span class='line-break'> </span> burn them.  If I did<span class='line-break'> </span> it would not trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> no one else and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children would not<span class='line-break'> </span> let them alone and<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie did not care.  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1218">
<h3><a name="page-1218">Saturday April  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  A big <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7721' title='hauling stalks'>hauled stalks</a> this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> after a <a href='../subjects/7698' title='dogs'>hound</a><span class='line-break'> </span> They went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid here and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a> to <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> caught 4 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I one.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> come back by <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Went to the store.  <a href='../subjects/8106' title='Hubbard'>Hubbard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was not there.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie said she intended <span class='line-break'> </span> to go to <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmoth</a> tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a>.  Josie dressed<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> to send <span class='line-break'> </span> to Julia.  Love to all the children<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; grand children.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1219">
<h3><a name="page-1219">Sunday April  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  We all<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home until noon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/241' title='Mr Padget'>Mr Padget</a><span class='line-break'> </span> preached.  There was a <span class='line-break'> </span> big crowd.  I though <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home.  The <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got out of the <a href='../subjects/321' title='pasture'>pasture</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim found her and brough<span class='line-break'> </span> her home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/8107' title='Mr Oaks'>Mr Oaks</a> a primtive<span class='line-break'> </span> Babtist <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I am very sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span> He will be missed so <span class='line-break'> </span> much.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1220">
<h3><a name="page-1220">Monday April  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; the two<span class='line-break'> </span> little children and I to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  Josie and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children stoped at <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; I went to <a href='../subjects/8107' title='Mr Oaks'>Mr Oaks</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.  There was a large<span class='line-break'> </span> crowd there.  Elder Boaz<span class='line-break'> </span> talked at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and they sung a song at<span class='line-break'> </span> the grave.  Heard that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8109' title='Mrs Walter Mills'>Mrs Mills</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  She was at her<span class='line-break'> </span> sisters when she died.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> today.  They stopped at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and they eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> there.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1221">
<h3><a name="page-1221">Tuesday April  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim made a <a href='../subjects/7748' title='hot bed'>hot bed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Had a nice dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> for this time of year.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a little.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> come this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I was very glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see her.  I wish they<span class='line-break'> </span> would come often.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes late this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had <span class='line-break'> </span> washed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> and come<span class='line-break'> </span> back by the store.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Two men come here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They wanted to <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>put<span class='line-break'> </span> lights</a> in the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1222">
<h3><a name="page-1222">Wednesday April  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and done a round[?] as<span class='line-break'> </span> usual.  We went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> makeing <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> a <a href='../subjects/8079' title='suit'>suit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie worked <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklins</a> clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> while she was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie baked <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>light bread</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmot</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8109' title='Mrs Walter Mills'>Mrs Walter Mills</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield traded a <a href='../subjects/8027' title='typewriter'>type<span class='line-break'> </span> writer</a> for and <a href='../subjects/8111' title='organ'>organ to grind</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim made <a href='../subjects/7748' title='hot bed'>hot bed</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1223">
<h3><a name="page-1223">Thursday April  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.  Jim plowed<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> for her.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the first time this year.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8112' title='petticoats'>pettie coat</a>.  Finished it<span class='line-break'> </span> ready to wear.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  I staid there<span class='line-break'> </span> until they come back.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna staid to take <span class='line-break'> </span> care of <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1224">
<h3><a name="page-1224">Friday April  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> for Sunday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some and Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> has cried a lot <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I have not seen any<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> people today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I miss them.  There has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> less passing today than<span class='line-break'> </span> usual.  I have not seen <span class='line-break'> </span> a car pass today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1225">
<h3><a name="page-1225">Saturday April  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> have his <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>teeth worked on</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got his worke done.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a silk <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a> for Jim.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> have a nice bed of salit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have bin at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day and no one come.<span class='line-break'> </span> Was thinkin that <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a><span class='line-break'> </span> might come.  Hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> will come soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1226">
<h3><a name="page-1226">Sunday April 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this morning.  Clear <span class='line-break'> </span> and very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a> this morning.  We all<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening except <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  A <a href='../subjects/8113' title='Mr Upshaw'>Mr Upshaw</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8114' title='lecturing'>lectured</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> to a large crowd.<span class='line-break'> </span> His talk was fine<span class='line-break'> </span> I thought.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a lot of <span class='line-break'> </span> people there that I know<span class='line-break'> </span> but I did not speak <span class='line-break'> </span> to many of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today was <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  Josie had a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> filled with <a href='../subjects/8115' title='pineapples'>pine<span class='line-break'> </span> apple</a>.  It is fine.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1227">
<h3><a name="page-1227">Monday April 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Vegetation was partly<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8116' title='freeze'>frozen</a>.  All tender things<span class='line-break'> </span> was bitten by the colde.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/985' title='mauling'>mauled</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> straitened up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Josie went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> came to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> She brought <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I a <a href='../subjects/7861' title='bonnets'>bonnets</a>.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> of mine for I needed it.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1228">
<h3><a name="page-1228">Tuesday April 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A big <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> made me a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> store.  Come<span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a> to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> looks<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred</a> is a fine<span class='line-break'> </span> childe.  They had a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and tonight. <span class='line-break'> </span> The children was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening. Ben &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone tonight. Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and I and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today is the last day<span class='line-break'> </span> of this term.  <a href='../subjects/8117' title='Gordon McCormick'>Gordon McCormic</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Mrs Sallie Blair</a>, <a href='../subjects/8118' title='Evelyn Hutcherson'>Mrs Evylin<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8119' title='Eliz Porter'>Miss <span class='line-break'> </span> Eliz Porter</a> was the teacher.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1229">
<h3><a name="page-1229">Wednesday April 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home and worked.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>Turkey</a> eggs<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> eggs<span class='line-break'> </span> for Jim.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We come home.  Josie had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> a bout done.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> eat and Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; Franklin<span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>to fish</a>.  I did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing.  Henry caught<span class='line-break'> </span> one fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie made Edna a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7558' title='Jane Wooding'>Mrs Wooding</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I know I had<span class='line-break'> </span> better stay at home and<span class='line-break'> </span> help do the work but am<span class='line-break'> </span> so trifling that I dont do what<span class='line-break'> </span> I should do.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1230">
<h3><a name="page-1230">Thursday April 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain<span class='line-break'> </span> until night.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled old rails</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> stove wood.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> then got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/8075' title='sowing grass'>sowed</a> some.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had washed.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope he will get well<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.  I went to the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed</a> and cut <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner tomorrows<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1231">
<h3><a name="page-1231">Friday April 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the island for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  Carried a log<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  She baked <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>light<span class='line-break'> </span> rolls</a> for supper.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that he come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim has a very bad<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  I am sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1232">
<h3><a name="page-1232">Saturday April 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cloudy day no rain<span class='line-break'> </span> until night. Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> hauled old rails fa <span class='line-break'></span> [?hove?] wood.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> then got dinner &amp; churned<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie sewed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening. I went to [?marvins?]<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie had washed. Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> is very much complaining<span class='line-break'> </span> hope he will get well<span class='line-break'> </span> Soon I went to the plant <span class='line-break'> </span> bed and cut salit<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. Tomorrows<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1233">
<h3><a name="page-1233">Sunday April 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until noon.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> and I walked to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a>.  He brough<span class='line-break'> </span> us home on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred</a> come with<span class='line-break'> </span> us home but did not<span class='line-break'> </span> get out of the car.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The weather has turned<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> and the <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is blowing to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1234">
<h3><a name="page-1234">Monday April 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day rained most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the evening and still raining.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went to Chatham<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin carried him. Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went for [Guave] carried<span class='line-break'> </span> a log to the mill.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> John went to see Corrie<span class='line-break'> </span> a [] this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> John and henry went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Strail Stone this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went horse back.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had fried chicken<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner. The first that<span class='line-break'> </span> we had killed this<span class='line-break'> </span> spring. To night is a<span class='line-break'> </span> [??ny] bad time on little<span class='line-break'> </span> chickens hope it will<span class='line-break'> </span> quit raining soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1235">
<h3><a name="page-1235">Tuesday April 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>Colde</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> April.  A big <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> island for <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  Got<span class='line-break'> </span> home by <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Carried<span class='line-break'> </span> some guano.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made her a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I got dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come.  We were <span class='line-break'> </span> very glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I walked with them <span class='line-break'> </span> as far as <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1236">
<h3><a name="page-1236">Wednesday April 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/8120' title='fencing'>fenced</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7505' title='disking'>disked</a> some and <a href='../subjects/8098' title='harrowing'>harrowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I built<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> coop.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> cut <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  Heard this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is bad off.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> sorry.  I think so well<span class='line-break'> </span> of her.  She is a good<span class='line-break'> </span> neighbor.  I think she<span class='line-break'> </span> tries to do as good as she<span class='line-break'> </span> can.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1237">
<h3><a name="page-1237">Thursday April 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/8098' title='harrowing'>harrowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/8120' title='fencing'>fenced</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then<span class='line-break'> </span> her and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> come to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Today was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> birth day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a> invited several<span class='line-break'> </span> of the kinsfolk to come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was all that went for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Christinia went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the store and bought <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and lemmons.  Made <a href='../subjects/7834' title='lemonaide'>lemon<span class='line-break'> </span> aid</a> and served cakes &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> aid.  Mollie has children<span class='line-break'> </span> that she is proud of.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> seem to think so much of<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>his mother</a> and sister up<span class='line-break'> </span> there this evening and come and<span class='line-break'> </span> brough us all home.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there two.  I enjoyed it all.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1238">
<h3><a name="page-1238">Friday April 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> just at night.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked all day at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> carried us.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> all day and<span class='line-break'> </span> did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing.<span class='line-break'> </span> We eat dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> at <a href='../subjects/7713' title='Mr Peak'>Mr Peaks</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr and <a href='../subjects/7863' title='Mrs Peak'>Mrs Peak</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> very nice to me and I<span class='line-break'> </span> am very glad for any<span class='line-break'> </span> kindness that is to me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Mr Irvin Lewis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8122' title='Irvin Lewis Mother'>his mother</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> fishing.  <a href='../subjects/8123' title='Les Roark'>Mr Less Rourks</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> us home.  I hope I have<span class='line-break'> </span> not done any harm to any<span class='line-break'> </span> one to day.  If so excuse me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1239">
<h3><a name="page-1239">Saturday April 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day except early morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar Brumfield</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> here for <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> help him work on it.<span class='line-break'> </span> They worked on it until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve and after then<span class='line-break'> </span> Oscar carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>to fish</a>.  The river was<span class='line-break'> </span> very mudy.  I caught 3 <span class='line-break'> </span> fish and Oscar caught<span class='line-break'> </span> five.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried him to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Henry went with<span class='line-break'> </span> Hugh home to spend the <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  There was a <a href='../subjects/7437' title='farm sale'>sale</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/8124' title='Mrs Creasy'>Mrs Creasys</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  None of my folks<span class='line-break'> </span> went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> <a href='../subjects/7789' title='swarming'>swarmed</a>.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> hived them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1240">
<h3><a name="page-1240">Sunday April 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and family except <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Powers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/200' title='Richard Wooding'>Richard Wooding</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Hubbards.  Went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> trap but did<span class='line-break'> </span> not get any fish.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got home at dark.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  They went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harveys</a>.  I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Kate had company.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wigginton</a> and <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> and <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen Brumfield</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8043' title='Virginia Moses'>Miss Virginia Moses</a>, two <span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/8125' title='Farmer children'>Farmer children</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I come home and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Brought <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> and made<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7474' title='baking bread'>baked bread</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1241">
<h3><a name="page-1241">Monday April 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  Jim come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  The men that will<span class='line-break'> </span> put in the <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>lights</a> come today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to the island.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got his <a href='../subjects/8127' title='washing machine'>washing machine</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a>.  I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> to the island.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Beaula</a> and I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  Did<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> at <a href='../subjects/7713' title='Mr Peak'>Mr Peaks</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are all so good to me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am ashamed to impose<span class='line-break'> </span> on them.  I thanked Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> for takeing me to the island. Got stuck<span class='line-break'> </span> in the mud between <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and the gray soil road.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7550' title='Jesse Hutcherson'>Mr Hutcherson</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> to push his <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a> out.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1242">
<h3><a name="page-1242">Tuesday April 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  A <a href='../subjects/314' title='thunder cloud'>thunder cloud</a> now<span class='line-break'> </span> at 8 oclock.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and worked it with the hoe.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> washed with their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8127' title='washing machine'>new washer</a>.  They are pleased<span class='line-break'> </span> with it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and the children all<span class='line-break'> </span> but <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie washed the dineing<span class='line-break'> </span> room floor be fore she went.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried Edna and I<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  I caught<span class='line-break'> </span> three <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Reese caught<span class='line-break'> </span> one.  There was at least<span class='line-break'> </span> a dozen people at <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I guess all had a good time if<span class='line-break'> </span> they did not get many fish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/7541' title='Mt. Airy, Virginia'>Mt Airy</a> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> closed to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1243">
<h3><a name="page-1243">Wednesday April 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  We had rain<span class='line-break'> </span> and lightning and <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a><span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has bin <a href='../subjects/8128' title='blasting stumps'>blowing up stumps</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7541' title='Mt. Airy, Virginia'>Mt Airy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for fuse and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the children went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We cooked <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and turnips.<span class='line-break'> </span> We looked for the men that<span class='line-break'> </span> is to put in <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>lights</a> but<span class='line-break'> </span> they did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> makeing <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> was at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> to day.
