She had bin<span class='line-break'> </span> doing some fancy work for<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie.  Josie fixed a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> towel this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1244">
<h3><a name="page-1244">Thursday April 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/8128' title='blasting stumps'>got up stumps</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and went to the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant<span class='line-break'> </span> bed</a> and got <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrows <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> a gown<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> whle I<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> has put<span class='line-break'> </span> stiches on two of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazels</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dresses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and will put some on<span class='line-break'> </span> Evas.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> got some papers.<span class='line-break'> </span> He sent <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> two.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today was <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> birthday.  She is 56.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1245">
<h3><a name="page-1245">Friday April 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> folks could not do much<span class='line-break'> </span> of any thing.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>to fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was people there seining.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a little in the pond.<span class='line-break'> </span> A cloud began to gather <span class='line-break'> </span> and I was a fraid to stay<span class='line-break'> </span> so we come home and then <span class='line-break'> </span> it did not rain much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> closed at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> this evening.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> a big crowd there.  We did<span class='line-break'> </span> not stop there.  <a href='../subjects/7458' title='Mrs Anderson'>Mrs Anderson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7327' title='Mrs Blair'>Mrs Blair</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7280' title='Hubbards'>Hubbards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> store and got a nice lot of <span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  Josie fried some for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I did not eat any to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1246">
<h3><a name="page-1246">Saturday April 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>stove</a> wood this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He broke his <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a> and borrowed <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7283' title='Bob Starkey'>Mr Bob Starkeys</a> to saw his<span class='line-break'> </span> wood.  <a href='../subjects/8129' title='Mr Woodall'>Mr Woodall</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> helped him.  They had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> for the <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>rools</a> for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> day today.  I am a fraid<span class='line-break'> </span> that the frost will kill<span class='line-break'> </span> all tender things tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1247">
<h3><a name="page-1247">Sunday May  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> bad day.  Not <span class='line-break'> </span> any thing was hurt by the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> started<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried her to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a> <a href='../subjects/8133' title='Mr Street'>Mr Street</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/241' title='Mr Padget'>Mr Padget</a> preached.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was a good many<span class='line-break'> </span> to hear him.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim staid a round here all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1248">
<h3><a name="page-1248">Monday May  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/7337' title='tobacco ground'>tobacco ground</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> wet a lot of <a href='../subjects/8134' title='gingham'>gingham</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> it this evening.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/241' title='Mr Padget'>Mr Padget</a><span class='line-break'> </span> even taken me and gave me a ride.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad of it.  Found all well<span class='line-break'> </span> at Mags.  I come by <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8106' title='Hubbard'>Hubbard</a> was <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Hubbard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was freezing <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.  I then come<span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols's</a>.  There was no one at<span class='line-break'> </span> home but <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> and children the<span class='line-break'> </span> rest of them was gone to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> went with them.  I come<span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/435' title='James Farthing'>Mr Farthings</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8135' title='Mrs Farthing'>Mrs Farthing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has nice little girl a week olde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Her name is <a href='../subjects/8136' title='Elsie Farthing'>Elsie May</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a lot of company.  I then<span class='line-break'> </span> come by Marvins and then<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Josie had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a bout ready.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1249">
<h3><a name="page-1249">Tuesday May  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  Have<span class='line-break'> </span> needed <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fires</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/7337' title='tobacco ground'>tobacco ground</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> roofing for the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> shelters.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Ben carried <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made Henry two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirts</a> and two pair of <a href='../subjects/7356' title='curtains'>curtains</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> this  morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was makeing<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard of several <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> today.  It is very<span class='line-break'> </span> early to plant yet it <span class='line-break'> </span> may do well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1250">
<h3><a name="page-1250">Wednesday May  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to day.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> did not come back.  Ben got<span class='line-break'> </span> home a bout dark.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She baked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.  They were fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  Jims <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>games</a><span class='line-break'> </span> began to hatch today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> will sleep with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> to night down<span class='line-break'> </span> stairs.  Edna will sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> with me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I want the weather<span class='line-break'> </span> to get good so bad.  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1251">
<h3><a name="page-1251">Thursday May  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The men that<span class='line-break'> </span> was to put in <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>the light</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come and worked all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They got one so we<span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> by it.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I hemed a pair<span class='line-break'> </span> of sheets.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes. To<span class='line-break'> </span> day was <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Evas</a> birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  She is three years olde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jims little <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>game chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hatched out today and yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> One of my <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> quit her<span class='line-break'> </span> nest.  I am sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am so glad that he come<span class='line-break'> </span> all right.  It is a discouraging<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I do hope that the<span class='line-break'> </span> weather will soon<span class='line-break'> </span> be better.  Then people will<span class='line-break'> </span> feel better I hope.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1252">
<h3><a name="page-1252">Friday May  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  The men finished puting<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>lights</a> and went home<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went two.  He went on<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Car and <a href='../subjects/8138' title='Mr Hobson'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Hobson</a> come with <span class='line-break'> </span> them home.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  Josie wanted<span class='line-break'> </span> her uncle to come<span class='line-break'> </span> so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8139' title='Woodall'>Woodall</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia F</a> and <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred</a> was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1253">
<h3><a name="page-1253">Saturday May  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has not<span class='line-break'> </span> done any work today.  Staid<span class='line-break'> </span> around with <a href='../subjects/8138' title='Mr Hobson'>Mr Hobson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and family went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> anything worth anything.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> attended to the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1254">
<h3><a name="page-1254">Sunday May  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8138' title='Mr Hobson'>Mr Hobson</a> is here yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> We cooked <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and fried two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  No one come <span class='line-break'> </span> to see us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Don't know any thing to write.<span class='line-break'> </span> I talked with <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> to night.  Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> hear anything new worth<span class='line-break'> </span> writing.  <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie</a> was to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them today.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is at home to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1255">
<h3><a name="page-1255">Monday May  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7923' title='hauling corn'>hauled</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/8140' title='Mr Young'>Mr Young</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> light man come this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come with him.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> helped Young fix up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8110' title='electricity'>lights</a>.  He finished here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> hatched<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I hived a swarm<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> this morning and<span class='line-break'> </span> then they went a way.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mending</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Jims <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1256">
<h3><a name="page-1256">Tuesday May 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> and I and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> and I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a little.<span class='line-break'> </span> By the kindness of <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> I got to go.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are very good to<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  Mrs Car and<span class='line-break'> </span> I stoped at <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mount<span class='line-break'> </span> Airy</a> and <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> paid up for the <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Edna has come to go <span class='line-break'> </span> to bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1257">
<h3><a name="page-1257">Wednesday May 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  We both<span class='line-break'> </span> got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am afraid<span class='line-break'> </span> they got wet before they<span class='line-break'> </span> got home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wanted to go to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> but went to the kitchen<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is <a href='../subjects/9420' title='raining'>raining</a> hard now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nine oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack Harvey</a> come a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1258">
<h3><a name="page-1258">Thursday May 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some tobacco today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  She went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a> for <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salit</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and lettice that<span class='line-break'> </span> was large enough to use.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1259">
<h3><a name="page-1259">Friday May 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and his crowd<span class='line-break'> </span> helped.  <a href='../subjects/8138' title='Mr Hobson'>Mr Hobson</a> left<span class='line-break'> </span> here today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some and made a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I put <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with Jims <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey hen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I finished <span class='line-break'> </span> the little girls pillow<span class='line-break'> </span> slips this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> carried them home.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> shot a crow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1260">
<h3><a name="page-1260">Saturday May 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> he carried me to <a href='../subjects/8141' title='Straightstone Creek'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone Creek</a> and the store.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come back by <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We met with <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane Reynols</a>.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  He had his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>teeth worked on</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Uncle Johnsons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  He got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8142' title='guinea hen'>guina</a> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.  I put them<span class='line-break'> </span> under a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>hen</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope that they may<span class='line-break'> </span> hatch.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried my <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8143' title='Peggy'>Peggy</a> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/321' title='pasture'>pasture</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1261">
<h3><a name="page-1261">Sunday May 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Car</a> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid here and looked <span class='line-break'> </span> after the things here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> met Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  He got home <span class='line-break'> </span> by night.  I met <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  He was lookin<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane Reynols</a> &amp; the <span class='line-break'> </span> boy come and staid a<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I wish Clifton well<span class='line-break'> </span> in his new home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I miss seeing <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> She went to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1262">
<h3><a name="page-1262">Monday May 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning.  Clear <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7737' title='hauling manure'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> manure</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> They fixed up some land<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made two <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirts</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> done some other things.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 4 of Jims <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a> drowned<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am so sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> about it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin bought a <a href='../subjects/453' title='pig'>pig</a> to day<span class='line-break'> </span> and two for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1263">
<h3><a name="page-1263">Tuesday May 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> fixed <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7790' title='dropping plants'>dropped plants</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  We had a big<span class='line-break'> </span> washing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> us this evening.  I was very<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> invited me to spend<span class='line-break'> </span> the day with her.  I could<span class='line-break'> </span> not go as we had<span class='line-break'> </span> commenced to wash.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard that <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny Emerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a> to <a href='../subjects/8144' title='Dews Leneir'>Dews Leneir</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I wish the childe well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1264">
<h3><a name="page-1264">Wednesday May 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on their <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> scrubed floors and<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie Smith</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see us this evening.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> not at home.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7854' title='Worshams pond'>Mr Worshams pond</a>.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  Caught a few.  Had<span class='line-break'> </span> a pleasant day.  Come by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbards</a><span class='line-break'> </span> baby was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was gone to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben did not like for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> to go with me.  Said<span class='line-break'> </span> he wanted him to work.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry to ever do<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing that makes him<span class='line-break'> </span> mad.  An old <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>hen</a> killed<span class='line-break'> </span> one of <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am very sorry that it<span class='line-break'> </span> happen.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1265">
<h3><a name="page-1265">Thursday May 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> fixed a<span class='line-break'> </span> mellon patch and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> at <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a>.  I went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> went.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> Caught 4 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> all small.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and Edna &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Mabel was all at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> they come to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen</a> and <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins this evenin.<span class='line-break'> </span> The first time they have come<span class='line-break'> </span> this year.  Effie &amp; Hellen<span class='line-break'> </span> will stay all night at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> two bushels of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1266">
<h3><a name="page-1266">Friday May 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> done the<span class='line-break'> </span> planting.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> layed off the<span class='line-break'> </span> rows.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I worked over<span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> coops.  Helped<span class='line-break'> </span> get a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked a few button <span class='line-break'> </span> holes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> store.  She bought some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Cooked them for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  They were fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> got in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not do much damage.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1267">
<h3><a name="page-1267">Saturday May 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> windows and scrubed<span class='line-break'> </span> floors.  I done nothing as<span class='line-break'> </span> usual.  Josie baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> caught 19 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with us tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floid Reynols</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come here and<span class='line-break'> </span> ask <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> to go <a href='../subjects/8145' title='camping'>camping</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I dont like no such.  Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing nothing wont happen<span class='line-break'> </span> to them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1268">
<h3><a name="page-1268">Sunday May 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  We looked for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>my brother</a> and family.<span class='line-break'> </span> They did not come.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry.  I heard tonight that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7422' title='Mr. Edmons'>Mr. Edmons</a> is feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> better.  I am glad of <span class='line-break'> </span> that.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I dont know any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing to write.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Little Mabel</a> is not so well<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Hope she will soon be<span class='line-break'> </span> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1269">
<h3><a name="page-1269">Monday May 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7764' title='corn land'>corn land</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> is not<span class='line-break'> </span> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We had a<span class='line-break'> </span> good trip.  <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this morning a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes on busines.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caped a few <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw<span class='line-break'> </span> berries</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1270">
<h3><a name="page-1270">Tuesday May 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> enough for a season.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> the children <a href='../subjects/7790' title='dropping plants'>dropped plants</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> fretted for <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/8079' title='suit'>suit</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> An agent come here<span class='line-break'> </span> today and is at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  He is enlarging<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7266' title='photography'>pictures</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1271">
<h3><a name="page-1271">Wednesday May 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planting tobacco</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7790' title='dropping plants'>droped some plants</a>.  I did <span class='line-break'> </span> not drop or draw a plant<span class='line-break'> </span> for the first time in years.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am not glad of it.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> like to help where I can.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do a lot of what is to<span class='line-break'> </span> be done at the house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Poor little <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> is a <span class='line-break'> </span> task by her self.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that growed this year.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1272">
<h3><a name="page-1272">Thursday May 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this evening.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> island for a <a href='../subjects/8127' title='washing machine'>washing <span class='line-break'> </span> machine</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> and <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>little daughter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come and spent the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were glad to have them.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floid</a> come after them this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today is <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>William Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  I would be <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> invited me<span class='line-break'> </span> to go <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  I would<span class='line-break'> </span> of liked to go but it<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> so that we could<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Hope he will<span class='line-break'> </span> ask me to go a gain.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1273">
<h3><a name="page-1273">Friday May 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day but no<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried him to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to Gretna with<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> finished <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> today.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> for him.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> washed <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and baked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a> for Sunday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/8147' title='garage'>garage</a> floor<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  It did help<span class='line-break'> </span> the looks so much.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1274">
<h3><a name="page-1274">Saturday May 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds about this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening but no rain to wet any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> and got some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> for tomorrows <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> killed and dressed three<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>, baked two <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> got dinner, and bathed<span class='line-break'> </span> the children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/7854' title='Worshams pond'>Worshams pond</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>to fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a>.  He went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> and had work<span class='line-break'> </span> done on his <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>teeth worked on</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I stoped at <a href='../subjects/8148' title='Jim Booker'>Mr Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Bookers</a> and sit on the<span class='line-break'> </span> porch with <a href='../subjects/7966' title='Mrs Booker'>Mrs Booker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> until Marvin come for us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <sensitive>I have felt all day that I<span class='line-break'> </span> was not doing right but I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> I may be forgiven.  I no<span class='line-break'> </span> longer boss things at our house</sensitive>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1275">
<h3><a name="page-1275">Sunday May 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> family and I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to a meeting<span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>Odd Fellows</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>sermond</a> and <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Every one seemed to have<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time.  <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come down.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben met him at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was at <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They had a lot of<span class='line-break'> </span> company mostly kindsfolks<span class='line-break'> </span> With all I think every<span class='line-break'> </span> one had as pleasant a <span class='line-break'> </span> time as could be expected.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are all at home<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight and all reasonable <span class='line-break'> </span> well.  I have a pain in <span class='line-break'> </span> my hip that hurts very<span class='line-break'> </span> bad at times.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1276">
<h3><a name="page-1276">Monday May 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> No rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> help.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not get up the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.  Could not find<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Hope that it will <span class='line-break'> </span> not rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie dressed two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night for <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1277">
<h3><a name="page-1277">Tuesday May 31, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home and worked.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and made some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>.  Greased the <span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.  I got the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the fowls.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then Stuart <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> for me and carried me to <span class='line-break'> </span> his home then <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr. Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried me to <a href='../subjects/8149' title='Owens mill'>Owens<span class='line-break'> </span> mill</a>.  We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> but did not<span class='line-break'> </span> catch much.  I did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing.  We had a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/7752' title='Lottie Kellie'>Lottie Kellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/8150' title='Mrs Owen'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> had enough to <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the crowd.  I had a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We all put our dinner together.<span class='line-break'> </span> I want to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> very<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1278">
<h3><a name="page-1278">Wednesday June  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she starched<span class='line-break'> </span> the clothes and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most<span class='line-break'> </span> of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They carried <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  The miller<span class='line-break'> </span> could not grind it but <span class='line-break'> </span> swaped <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a> for the corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> some.  Caught<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Stopped at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mount Airy</a> and at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  They carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred Fergerson</a> with them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1279">
<h3><a name="page-1279">Thursday June  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day or nearly all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.  All raised in<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have suffered some with<span class='line-break'> </span> my hip nearly a week.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that I am<span class='line-break'> </span> able to go as well as I<span class='line-break'> </span> can.  Do hope it will<span class='line-break'> </span> soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1280">
<h3><a name="page-1280">Friday June  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/8151' title='Hubbard&apos;s store'>Hubbard's store</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  He carried three<span class='line-break'> </span> of the children with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  This evening I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Thought<span class='line-break'> </span> I might get to go to the<span class='line-break'> </span> store but <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> was so<span class='line-break'> </span> busy that he could not<span class='line-break'> </span> go.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carry</a> was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for her self.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got done his little[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> crop of tobacco.  Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> they <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> get Jims<span class='line-break'> </span> done tomorrow.  We have <span class='line-break'> </span> a good <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> for this <span class='line-break'> </span> time of the year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is reading and<span class='line-break'> </span> it will soon be 10 oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1281">
<h3><a name="page-1281">Saturday June  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.  This<span class='line-break'> </span> evening Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Three of the children went<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went.  I bought<span class='line-break'> </span> a pair of <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a> and a <span class='line-break'> </span> few other things.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all the time that we<span class='line-break'> </span> were comeing home.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not get wet.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> bough ready when we <span class='line-break'> </span> got home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1282">
<h3><a name="page-1282">Sunday June  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>The boys stayed at home<span class='line-break'> </span> until late this evening then<span class='line-break'> </span> they went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Brother Letcher</a> and <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Ernest</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come this morning.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> Lottie this evening.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that they come.  Letcher<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me to <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim Bennetts</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I left <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> uneasy a bout her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1283">
<h3><a name="page-1283">Monday June  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I am at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Bennetts</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lony</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> are <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> is working<span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for <a href='../subjects/8152' title='Bessie Shelhorse'>Bessie<span class='line-break'> </span> Shelhorse</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> had English<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> firs that I have seen this<span class='line-break'> </span> year.  <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and brough his<span class='line-break'> </span> baby.  Lizzie &amp; Alma<span class='line-break'> </span> kept it until twelve<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock.  Well I do wish<span class='line-break'> </span> I could know how they<span class='line-break'> </span> are getting on at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> better off by now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1284">
<h3><a name="page-1284">Tuesday June  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning but no<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  I am haveing an easy<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  My hip hurts me<span class='line-break'> </span> some yet I worked two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> and hemed<span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilts</a> and gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some but they<span class='line-break'> </span> need rain bad.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7233' title='irrigation'>watered</a> their plant<span class='line-break'> </span> beds to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> went visiting<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> attends to the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  She has five<span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.  They are<span class='line-break'> </span> getting on fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I certainly do want <span class='line-break'> </span> to know how they are<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  Hope I will <span class='line-break'> </span> hear soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1285">
<h3><a name="page-1285">Wednesday June  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain<span class='line-break'> </span> to do any good.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> overalls.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some cloth this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a> and <a href='../subjects/8153' title='Shirley James Bennett'>the<span class='line-break'> </span> boy</a> come over here this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I walked to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a note from<span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to get it.  They said<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> was some better<span class='line-break'> </span> when they <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a>.  I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope that the children<span class='line-break'> </span> will keep well and<span class='line-break'> </span> all of the rest of them.<span class='line-break'> </span> I feel anxious a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout them all and<span class='line-break'> </span> my self two.  I hope my<span class='line-break'> </span> leg will soon be well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1286">
<h3><a name="page-1286">Thursday June  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> at Tims <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7569' title='garments'>garments</a>.  Lizzies washer<span class='line-break'> </span> woman brought her clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
