<p> <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim Bennett</a> has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>farmers meeting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> Bennett come<span class='line-break'> </span> over here today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote a letter</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home to night.  Hope<span class='line-break'> </span> they may get it soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1287">
<h3><a name="page-1287">Friday June 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted tobacco</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> sowed <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and peas for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> sowed some.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> two <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirts</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for the boys.  I cut<span class='line-break'> </span> some clover for Lizzies<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.  I had rather<span class='line-break'> </span> do something like that<span class='line-break'> </span> than set all the time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Alma had a note from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> this morning.  He will<span class='line-break'> </span> not be at home Sunday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Oh how bad I want<span class='line-break'> </span> to know a bout them<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  Want to see <span class='line-break'> </span> them all at home and<span class='line-break'> </span> of the rest of them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1288">
<h3><a name="page-1288">Saturday June 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  Had a<span class='line-break'> </span> little rain this evening.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> was badly needed and they<span class='line-break'> </span> need more so bad.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> boys here <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and Louise<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening after the <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  We had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> trip.  I bought a pair of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a> and good to make<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  We got  home<span class='line-break'> </span> early enough to do<span class='line-break'> </span> the work ok.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Mr Bennett</a> has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>farmers meeting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are fixin to go to bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1289">
<h3><a name="page-1289">Sunday June 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7259' title='Whittles Depot, Virginia'>Whittles</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a> and I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with them from<span class='line-break'> </span> Whittles to <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Tim &amp; Gordon<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Lonnie &amp; Lizzie and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/8154' title='Dr Mease'>Dr Meases</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Tenia</a> and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> rest of them.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> have a nice house.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to get to<span class='line-break'> </span> go.  There is a entertainment<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/8155' title='Oak Grove Christian Church'>Oak Grove church</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I could of gone but<span class='line-break'> </span> did not want to go so<span class='line-break'> </span> Alma and Lonnie went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1290">
<h3><a name="page-1290">Monday June 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> brought me to <a href='../subjects/7441' title='Joseph Terry Towler'>Jo Towlers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with brother Jo &amp; sister<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Mary</a>.  After ward we <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/8156' title='Billy Bennett'>Billie Bennetts</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were well over<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  I want to be<span class='line-break'> </span> at home so bad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1291">
<h3><a name="page-1291">Tuesday June 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very hot.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> need rain so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid at brother <a href='../subjects/7441' title='Joseph Terry Towler'>Joes</a> until<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>sister Mary</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to brother<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7445' title='John Craddock'>Johns</a>.  They were all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a> <a href='../subjects/8157' title='John Motley'>John Motley</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> the first time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8158' title='Annie Pickerel'>Annie Pickerel</a> made<span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> all enjoyed it very<span class='line-break'> </span> much.  I lost my side<span class='line-break'> </span> comes this morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1292">
<h3><a name="page-1292">Wednesday June 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I was at <a href='../subjects/7441' title='Joseph Terry Towler'>Jo<span class='line-break'> </span> Towler</a> this morning.  Sister<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not see <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Earnest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They have two nice little<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  Irvins wife<span class='line-break'> </span> and baby come to Earnest. <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at Letchers then he<span class='line-break'> </span> brought me to <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennetts</a>.  I am glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to be at Tims tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1293">
<h3><a name="page-1293">Thursday June 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> tried to cut<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> today but the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7824' title='binder'>binder</a> would not work.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> and <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a><span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> with home<span class='line-break'> </span> folks to night. Lonnie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Earl are in the<span class='line-break'> </span> hayfield now, nine<span class='line-break'> </span> oclock at night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Earl saw <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> going to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> for repairs for the<span class='line-break'> </span> binder.  I do hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> they got them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I would like to be<span class='line-break'> </span> at home tonight.  Every one<span class='line-break'> </span> is as kind to me as<span class='line-break'> </span> they can be but I have<span class='line-break'> </span> bin gone long enough for<span class='line-break'> </span> this time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1294">
<h3><a name="page-1294">Friday June 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  It was badly needed.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys here got up some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a> and <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> and <a href='../subjects/8153' title='Shirley James Bennett'>Shirly</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> after the rain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a>.  She said that she<span class='line-break'> </span> might come for me<span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  I want it to rain<span class='line-break'> </span> and I want her to come<span class='line-break'> </span> two.  I know I cant have <span class='line-break'> </span> both.  I do want to go<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Guess I will<span class='line-break'> </span> have to go with Earl<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett Sunday.<span class='line-break'> </span> Will be glad to do that.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I do hope that nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> will happen to hinder<span class='line-break'> </span> me from going.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1295">
<h3><a name="page-1295">Saturday June 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> from <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and family come<span class='line-break'> </span> up there.  Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim staid.  I come home<span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  Marvin &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Will</a> and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7984' title='Emily Lyle Brumfield'>Emily</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was here when I got<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I dont feel like here<span class='line-break'> </span> is home any more.<span class='line-break'> </span> I may be mean to feel<span class='line-break'> </span> that way but I cant<span class='line-break'> </span> help it.  I feel that others<span class='line-break'> </span> think they are so smart<span class='line-break'> </span> that I am a mere nobody.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was so glad that<span class='line-break'> </span> they come for me so<span class='line-break'> </span> as to trouble no one<span class='line-break'> </span> else. Saturday night<span class='line-break'> </span> June the 18th 1921<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1296">
<h3><a name="page-1296">Sunday June 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> and part<span class='line-break'> </span> of the chldren spent the day<span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>Mildred Fergerson</a>, <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice Thomson</a> &amp; her<span class='line-break'> </span> children and <a href='../subjects/8159' title='Mrs. Kent'>Mrs. Kent</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all come to see Willie.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them all.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Hope I may see<span class='line-break'> </span> her soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1297">
<h3><a name="page-1297">Monday June 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>Bill</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home.  <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> brought him<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> cut some of <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> this evening.  Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went with Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Heard this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning that <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has a <a href='../subjects/8160' title='Caroline Ferguson'>little daughter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> born this morning.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  I have not seen<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> to day.  I certainly <span class='line-break'> </span> did want to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well things dont go like<span class='line-break'> </span> I want them to but<span class='line-break'> </span> I cant help my self.<span class='line-break'> </span> Will try and do the best<span class='line-break'> </span> that I can.  That is all I can do.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1298">
<h3><a name="page-1298">Tuesday June 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We need rain<span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> got done by twelve oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> He come home for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> two bushels<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> at <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> a big washing.  She washed<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> and went<span class='line-break'> </span> over to Bedford to visit<span class='line-break'> </span> the Reese homested.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1299">
<h3><a name="page-1299">Wednesday June 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Clear this morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  We are very glad<span class='line-break'> </span> of it.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7827' title='cutting oats'>cut oats</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8161' title='replanting'>Replanted tobacco</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim have gone to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to night to<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>farmers meeting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> washed a little.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin had the <a href='../subjects/8162' title='surveyor'>surveyor</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at his house to day<span class='line-break'> </span> to cut his land in lots<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/8163' title='land sale'>sell</a>.  I am very sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that he will sell but it<span class='line-break'> </span> may be for the best.<span class='line-break'> </span> I know I sall miss them<span class='line-break'> </span> if I live that long.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin has bin kind to me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1300">
<h3><a name="page-1300">Thursday June 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> went to night after <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to cap them.  They hope that<span class='line-break'> </span> it will rain by morning.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got up some <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>her baby</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; all of her children<span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to see Julia<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They had a lot<span class='line-break'> </span> of company.  <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a>, <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice Thomson</a> and all of her<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollies</a> but I did hear<span class='line-break'> </span> any news of importance.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1301">
<h3><a name="page-1301">Friday June 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got the <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> up &amp; stacked<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  It was a mighty hot <span class='line-break'> </span> job.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> thined some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children except <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> sent some corn.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>. <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8164' title='swimming'>went batheing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a><span class='line-break'> </span> waded in the <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span> We caught several small<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I did enjoy the<span class='line-break'> </span> trip.  <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladis</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8165' title='Hilda Brumfield'>Hildah Bru</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7562' title='Stuart Owen'>Stewart Owen</a> has fever.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope he may get <span class='line-break'> </span> well soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1302">
<h3><a name="page-1302">Saturday June 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> get up some <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> folks helped<span class='line-break'> </span> thin <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> until they finished.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I picked<span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a half gallon &amp; had all they<span class='line-break'> </span> would eat for dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I slept a long nap<span class='line-break'> </span> after dinner.  Something<span class='line-break'> </span> I dont often do.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well we are all glad of<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>good rain</a> that come<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> has come to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1303">
<h3><a name="page-1303">Sunday June 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  A little <span class='line-break'> </span> rain this evening.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> was here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> 4 of the boys were together<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We gave them a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a><span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I dont know any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing to write.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1304">
<h3><a name="page-1304">Monday June 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Ben did not stay long.<span class='line-break'> </span> Then he <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> plowed some and then<span class='line-break'> </span> mowed <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.  Them and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> have gone to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to hear <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>speakin</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <a href='../subjects/8166' title='peppers'>pepper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning then got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening she<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  Cut some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> peices and went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins.  Come home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fed &amp; milked.  Brought<span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/7252' title='buckets'>buckets</a> of <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1305">
<h3><a name="page-1305">Tuesday June 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> got<span class='line-break'> </span> up a little <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/8167' title='threshing machine'>thrashing<span class='line-break'> </span> machin</a> is at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> they <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> thought she would<span class='line-break'> </span> wash to day but it was<span class='line-break'> </span> late and so hot that <span class='line-break'> </span> she did not.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8071' title='Mrs Kent'>Mrs Kent</a> come by this <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> evening.  She had bin to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8168' title='Tom Lay'>Tom Lays</a> land<span class='line-break'> </span> was sold today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished reading a book<span class='line-break'> </span> tha <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> lone<span class='line-break'> </span> me.  Josie has commenced to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7626' title='reading'>read</a> it.  She is reading now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1306">
<h3><a name="page-1306">Wednesday June 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  The <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrashed</a> the <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> here this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  They were here for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Then <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got up some <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8139' title='Woodall'>Woodall</a> hauled some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a> for them.  It rain a<span class='line-break'> </span> little this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7558' title='Jane Wooding'>Mrs Wooding</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8170' title='James Wooding, Jr.'>her baby</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  There<span class='line-break'> </span> is a man there to night<span class='line-break'> </span> thinkin a bout buying<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins home tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin thinks so little <span class='line-break'> </span> of it that he is going<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/8163' title='land sale'>sell</a>.  Oh I am<span class='line-break'> </span> so sorry.  No knows but<span class='line-break'> </span> me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1307">
<h3><a name="page-1307">Thursday June 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished getting<span class='line-break'> </span> up <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a> and hauled up <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> solde his land<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a> bought<span class='line-break'> </span> it as Marvin would <a href='../subjects/8163' title='land sale'>sell</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had Norman had it as<span class='line-break'> </span> any one that I can think of.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh how I shall miss them<span class='line-break'> </span> if I live that long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come here a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> has cried a lot<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I am certain that she<span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7376' title='Virginia Wooding'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding</a> all went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to hear them sell.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>[?]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1308">
<h3><a name="page-1308">Friday July  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> finished getting<span class='line-break'> </span> up their <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a> and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some in the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a>[?] some today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  I did<span class='line-break'> </span> not stay long.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with someone.<span class='line-break'> </span> He sent me home on<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  He brought some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a>.  Carrie &amp; Josie made<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.  We had more then<span class='line-break'> </span> we could eat.  Ben &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a> some of the <span class='line-break'> </span> cream.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Last night a bout one in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning a bug got in<span class='line-break'> </span> my ear.  I could of cried if it<span class='line-break'> </span> would of done any good.  Got it<span class='line-break'> </span> out after 3 this a.m.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1309">
<h3><a name="page-1309">Saturday July  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A hot dry day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a> and got <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to cover the shelters at the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  This evening he covered<span class='line-break'> </span> one and would of covered<span class='line-break'> </span> the other one but I ask him<span class='line-break'> </span> to fix the trough at the<span class='line-break'> </span> kitchen door.  He did not want<span class='line-break'> </span> to do that but did it just <span class='line-break'> </span> the same.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she made her<span class='line-break'> </span> a waist.  <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>, <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> are all up stairs makeing<span class='line-break'> </span> so much fuss that I shall<span class='line-break'> </span> not go to bed until they<span class='line-break'> </span> stop. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1310">
<h3><a name="page-1310">Sunday July  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I am at <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber<span class='line-break'> </span> Jeffersons</a> to night.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me to the road where I<span class='line-break'> </span> met <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim</a> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a>, <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonny</a>, <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We come to Faber Jeffersons.<span class='line-break'> </span> Fond them all well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Have seen Mr &amp; <a href='../subjects/8171' title='Mrs Oaks'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Oaks</a>.  I was glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> see them.  I saw <a href='../subjects/8172' title='George Oaks'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> George</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8173' title='Will Oaks'>Will Oaks</a> at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladys</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Mr Bennett</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> Faber &amp; <a href='../subjects/8107' title='Mr Oaks'>Mr Oaks</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/7377' title='Jim Reynolds'>Jim Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1311">
<h3><a name="page-1311">Monday July  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good hot day.  I was at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber Jeffersons</a> in <a href='../subjects/8174' title='Charlotte County, Virginia'>Charloot<span class='line-break'> </span> County</a>.  The Bennett boys went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/8175' title='Red House, Virginia'>red house</a> to a <a href='../subjects/8176' title='baseball'>base<span class='line-break'> </span> ball</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola</a> and I did<span class='line-break'> </span> not go.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> went this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We started from the red house<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout 5 oclock.  I got home<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout sundown.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> was here when<span class='line-break'> </span> I got home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> done and had <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family except<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>the baby</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to see a <a href='../subjects/388' title='movie'>picture<span class='line-break'> </span> show</a>.  The baby staid a <span class='line-break'> </span> wake until they got home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad I am at<span class='line-break'> </span> home a gain.  Next time<span class='line-break'> </span> I go I want to go <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1312">
<h3><a name="page-1312">Tuesday July  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a> all the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  They got a fine lot.<span class='line-break'> </span> Nellie preserved hers.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> what she got.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/8177' title='Mr McNary'>Mr McNary</a>[?] is<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> None of my folks<span class='line-break'> </span> went to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to see <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>the show</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> wanted to go bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> The rest did not come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1313">
<h3><a name="page-1313">Wednesday July  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Jim helped pick<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a> this evening.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the shelters at<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  He went to <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack<span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbards</a> and got some <a href='../subjects/8178' title='nails'>nails</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/10661' title='sugar'>sugar</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> come on a <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>bycile</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> could not let it a lone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had washed today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some berries this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1314">
<h3><a name="page-1314">Thursday July  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> but not a drop<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  We need rain so bad.  <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> &amp; preserved some <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for us this morning.  She went<span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> her to Gretna.  I went with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Ben bought some <a href='../subjects/8179' title='ship stuff'>ship<span class='line-break'> </span> stuff</a> and <a href='../subjects/384' title='beet pulp'>beet pulp</a> for the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while.  <a href='../subjects/8129' title='Mr Woodall'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Woodall</a> left Marvins this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> &amp; I<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>the<span class='line-break'> </span> show</a> to night.  There was a<span class='line-break'> </span> big crowd.  It was good of<span class='line-break'> </span> its kind.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1315">
<h3><a name="page-1315">Friday July  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> colouds a round this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Very little rain here.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> need rain very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked in Jims<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come today.  John<span class='line-break'> </span> wanted to see <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a bout some land at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> by her<span class='line-break'> </span> self.  She had a good dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on<span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> have all<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1316">
<h3><a name="page-1316">Saturday July  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  It is needed so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was so low that they could<span class='line-break'> </span> no grind.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a fished caught two <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> by <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> am glad that she got it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> No one from here did not<span class='line-break'> </span> go to <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>the show</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is raining now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1317">
<h3><a name="page-1317">Sunday July 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain last night<span class='line-break'> </span> to do any good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve then eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went to <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Powers</a>.  Found them all<span class='line-break'> </span> well.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8181' title='Bessie Hobson'>Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Bessie Hobson</a> there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Jim &amp; Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> walked a bout all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They are so<span class='line-break'> </span> dissaisfied with their crop<span class='line-break'> </span> and cant help themselves.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8104' title='Emmet Brumfield'>Emmet Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> says that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7459' title='Asa Anderson'>Asa Anderson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> nine oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1318">
<h3><a name="page-1318">Monday July 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain yet to<span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  The boys worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished covering<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> shetter this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> got up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and made <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got up soon this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and made a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> &amp; brough a <span class='line-break'> </span> bucket of <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.  Washed <span class='line-break'> </span> last nights dishes then got the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> before any one else<span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I then <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Made a fire at the <a href='../subjects/7624' title='wash house'>wash house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and washed until twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Eat dinner and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>his mother</a> &amp; all the <span class='line-break'> </span> children.  The river was so mudy<span class='line-break'> </span> that we did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch anything</a> any<span class='line-break'> </span> acount.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1319">
<h3><a name="page-1319">Tuesday July 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain to do any<span class='line-break'> </span> good yet.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I am sorry for<span class='line-break'> </span> her to have such a time.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> washed and had her<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to get.  I am sorry<span class='line-break'> </span> that she has such a time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cant get help for any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some on<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Made one peice tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope to finish it soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1320">
<h3><a name="page-1320">Wednesday July 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain yet here.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben <a href='../subjects/8182' title='whitewashing'>white washed</a> the room<span class='line-break'> </span> that I sleep in.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made<span class='line-break'> </span> her a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7816' title='berries'>berries</a>.  Julia stuck a barb<span class='line-break'> </span> wire in her leg.  I hope it<span class='line-break'> </span> wont get sore much.  A <a href='../subjects/404' title='wasp'>wasp</a><span class='line-break'> </span> stung <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  I hope it<span class='line-break'> </span> wont hurt him long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Miss Fannie Power</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7459' title='Asa Anderson'>Mr Asa Anderson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7313' title='Piney Grove'>Piny Grove</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are carrieng on.<span class='line-break'> </span> Protracted <a href='../subjects/8183' title='revival meeting'>meeting</a> there<span class='line-break'> </span> this week.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1321">
<h3><a name="page-1321">Thursday July 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a> all the<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben finished the room<span class='line-break'> </span> that he was at work on<span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  Then he carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me and some of the children <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We had a <span class='line-break'> </span> good outing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1322">
<h3><a name="page-1322">Friday July 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  We are all glad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8184' title='Walter Owen'>Walter Owen</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  He was looking<span class='line-break'> </span> for a home for another<span class='line-break'> </span> year.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> him a little on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come with Marvin.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> were at <a href='../subjects/8185' title='Rowling&apos;s Store'>Rowling store</a><span class='line-break'> </span> when it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It sounds like the children<span class='line-break'> </span> will tear down the house<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1323">
<h3><a name="page-1323">Saturday July 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/7382' title='kitchen'>cook room</a><span class='line-break'> </span> walls all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fannie<span class='line-break'> </span> Power</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> let <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> take<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> anything much.  We had<span class='line-break'> </span> some trouble when we got to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  We found that we<span class='line-break'> </span> had left <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>Hughs shoes</a> so we went<span class='line-break'> </span> back and got them.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to get them.  <a href='../subjects/8186' title='Charles Anderson'>Mr Charles Anderson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped Reese with the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  I did<span class='line-break'> </span> thank him so much.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John B</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight.  I am always glad for<span class='line-break'> </span> him to come.  Fannie P and <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> to see a <a href='../subjects/8187' title='ball game'>ball game</a>.  I have finished<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> that I peiced for <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1324">
<h3><a name="page-1324">Sunday July 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> went away<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Hope he got home ok.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while.  He carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny</a> for spin and come<span class='line-break'> </span> back and then went to <a href='../subjects/7779' title='Mr Farmer'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Farmers</a> for <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went with us to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then come home and carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7859' title='Fannie'>Fannie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> to <a href='../subjects/7313' title='Piney Grove'>Piney Grove</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  I have just put<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> in her bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> up stairs to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am tiered.  It is hard to<span class='line-break'> </span> have to wait on folks<span class='line-break'> </span> that care nothing but a <span class='line-break'> </span> good time at some one else<span class='line-break'> </span> expence.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1325">
<h3><a name="page-1325">Monday July 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  They staid all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come with them<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; done the work.  <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charley<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> spent the evening with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fannie Power</a> at Aunt <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He carried her to church<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  I got the <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> then<span class='line-break'> </span> went <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried me.  <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went two.  We did not<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing but I<span class='line-break'> </span> will go a gain the first time<span class='line-break'> </span> I can get to go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard tonight that Capt Tate<span class='line-break'> </span> is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1326">
<h3><a name="page-1326">Tuesday July 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We need rain very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Richard Woodings</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and helped <a href='../subjects/8188' title='topping tobacco'>top his tobacco</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> thin <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  Richard is in a <a href='../subjects/7799' title='hospital'>hospittle</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was some 7 or 8 men to<span class='line-break'> </span> help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie &amp; <a href='../subjects/7859' title='Fannie'>Fannie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> all went to the store.<span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Ben &amp; Josie and Fannie<span class='line-break'> </span> and Julia has all gone to <a href='../subjects/7313' title='Piney Grove'>Piny<span class='line-break'> </span> Grove</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  I lost my <a href='../subjects/7987' title='glasses'>glasses</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had I put them in a<span class='line-break'> </span> book and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> carried them<span class='line-break'> </span> up stairs.  <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>Mr John Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and part of his family<span class='line-break'> </span> come to Marvins this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8189' title='Capt Tate'>Capt Tate</a> is <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1327">
<h3><a name="page-1327">Wednesday July 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening but no rain to do any<span class='line-break'> </span> good.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fannie Power</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/7459' title='Asa Anderson'>Ada Anderson</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> her and then carried her<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  We will miss her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Her and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went to the <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I cut a few <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> peices<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/8183' title='revival meeting'>meeting</a> at <a href='../subjects/7313' title='Piney Grove'>Piny Grove</a><span class='line-break'> </span> closed to day.  They had two<span class='line-break'> </span> sermons and dinner on the <span class='line-break'> </span> grounds.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Had <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> raised this year<span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1328">
<h3><a name="page-1328">Thursday July 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.
