We need rain very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all the morning. Worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> come up here today<span class='line-break'> </span> at noon and talked with<span class='line-break'> </span> the boys a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made two <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dresses</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  One for herself and<span class='line-break'> </span> one for <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Julia has gone to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Will stay a day or two.<span class='line-break'> </span> We will mis her very <span class='line-break'> </span> much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evenig.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> boys washed a<span class='line-break'> </span> washing of clothes to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1329">
<h3><a name="page-1329">Friday July 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked on tobacco</a> until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve oclock.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with some <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  Come<span class='line-break'> </span> by Edwards and got a <span class='line-break'> </span> load of <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> drove <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>Bens car</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and all the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch</a> but a<span class='line-break'> </span> few <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to look at some land near<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8191' title='Gladys, Virginia'>Gladys, Virginia</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8160' title='Caroline Ferguson'>baby</a>.  I want to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set a hen</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1330">
<h3><a name="page-1330">Saturday July 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain yet.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> it so bad.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has bin a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> the home most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7395' title='tomato patch'>tomato patch</a>.  They got a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> come from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols</a> come with her.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> spent most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> sent us a <span class='line-break'> </span> peice of <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made some <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was fine.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Ben has gone to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to night to<span class='line-break'> </span> a meeting of the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The first time in a long<span class='line-break'> </span> time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1331">
<h3><a name="page-1331">Sunday July 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>, <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a> to spend<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  This evening Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie &amp; Rob &amp; <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce</a> place in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8174' title='Charlotte County, Virginia'>Charlott Co</a>.  They went to<span class='line-break'> </span> look at the <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> grounds.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home &amp; <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and washed<span class='line-break'> </span> dishes and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> by myself to<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Then I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> did not have any<span class='line-break'> </span> company.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1332">
<h3><a name="page-1332">Monday July 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds about<span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain here.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on their<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> un til noon.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Jim and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to three stores<span class='line-break'> </span> hunting <a href='../subjects/8192' title='bolts'>bolts</a> for a <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> body.  To night Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/8193' title='lecture'>speaking</a>.  Josie &amp; I<span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I cut <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a><span class='line-break'> </span> peices this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry and I cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> up the olde <a href='../subjects/7903' title='stable'>stable</a> where<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> stais.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> has bin hemstichen<span class='line-break'> </span> on a peic for a ruffle.<span class='line-break'> </span> She gets on well for her<span class='line-break'> </span> first.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1333">
<h3><a name="page-1333">Tuesday July 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain here<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and on <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> body this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  The <a href='../subjects/8127' title='washing machine'>machine engine</a><span class='line-break'> </span> would not work.  She washed<span class='line-break'> </span> by hand.  This evening <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>her mother</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> staid all night.  Ben &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and Virginia &amp; <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> have all gone to Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to <a href='../subjects/8183' title='revival meeting'>meeting</a>.  Hope <span class='line-break'> </span> that they may have a<span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant time and no<span class='line-break'> </span> one get hurt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and her little ones<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin sent for them.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> brought the car.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8194' title='Thomas Thompson'>Thomas Tomson</a> brough Virginia home<span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1334">
<h3><a name="page-1334">Wednesday July 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain in sight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> they went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Staid all the evening.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got their <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> went home this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with her.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfields</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  I miss her very<span class='line-break'> </span> much.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning &amp; <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> spent most<span class='line-break'> </span> of their time playing in<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.  Marvin went<span class='line-break'> </span> with Ben &amp; Jim to the <span class='line-break'> </span> saw mill.  The land is so<span class='line-break'> </span> dry that <a href='../subjects/8195' title='suckers'>suckers</a> dont grow<span class='line-break'> </span> so the men are idle.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1335">
<h3><a name="page-1335">Thursday July 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  No rain yet.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> need it so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> put a new<span class='line-break'> </span> floor in the <a href='../subjects/8032' title='dining room'>dineing room</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad of it.  We eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> under the <a href='../subjects/8196' title='mulberry tree'>mulberrie<span class='line-break'> </span> tree</a>.  Some men come here<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7546' title='election'>electtionneering</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  I am glad he<span class='line-break'> </span> is well enough to go a <span class='line-break'> </span> round a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come a while<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  They went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> for dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> Guess they went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for to spend the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1336">
<h3><a name="page-1336">Friday July 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked on the tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning then floored<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7382' title='kitchen'>cook room</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> him then come home and<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>his mother</a> and all<span class='line-break'> </span> the children and I to <a href='../subjects/8197' title='Johnson&apos;s mill'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Johnsons mill</a>.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> waded<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout in <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> a little.  Caught four.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A man come here<span class='line-break'> </span> and bought 23 <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and two doz <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> are<span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight.  Bus [?] Miller<span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is the hand<span class='line-break'> </span> that worked at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> broke the shade<span class='line-break'> </span> trees.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1337">
<h3><a name="page-1337">Saturday July 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> but none here to do any<span class='line-break'> </span> good.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> and washed and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked for her self and <span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to the <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>meeting<span class='line-break'> </span> of the farmers</a> at the <a href='../subjects/8198' title='experiment station'>experiment <span class='line-break'> </span> station</a> not far from <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was a big crowd and<span class='line-break'> </span> lots of something to eat and<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8193' title='lecture'>speaking</a>.  If every one did <span class='line-break'> </span> not get enough to eat it was<span class='line-break'> </span> their no trying to get it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Met several of my kindsfolks<span class='line-break'> </span> and friends that I once<span class='line-break'> </span> knew.  We come to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> and staid a lone time.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> hard.  It is raining<span class='line-break'> </span> here now.  I hope that it<span class='line-break'> </span> may rain enough to get<span class='line-break'> </span> the land wet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1338">
<h3><a name="page-1338">Sunday July 31, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> All of the children went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  They come by <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a> and <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> with them home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; was<span class='line-break'> </span> eating when they got here.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7465' title='St Andrews'>St Andrews</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a> and his wife<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a> come home with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Josie done the best<span class='line-break'> </span> she could for them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1339">
<h3><a name="page-1339">Monday August  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I got up and<span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes and <a href='../subjects/7587' title='cattle killing'>killed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/7810' title='cutting wheat'>cut</a> them<span class='line-break'> </span> up.  The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a> &amp; wife is<span class='line-break'> </span> very pleasant company.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went a way a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> 9 oclock this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come with him back.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> bought the Dollie Hays place<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Hope he may be<span class='line-break'> </span> satisfied with it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard Ben &amp; Jim tells a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout the <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>awful rain</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> they had at Gretna and the <span class='line-break'> </span> damage that it done.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry for them.  That was<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing that people could help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come here<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am going to see her soon if I<span class='line-break'> </span> keep able.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1340">
<h3><a name="page-1340">Tuesday August  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> was at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  He was a judge at<span class='line-break'> </span> an <a href='../subjects/7546' title='election'>election</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/8434' title='suckering tobacco'>sucker<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> carried his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> to vote.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1341">
<h3><a name="page-1341">Wednesday August  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Sprinkled rain<span class='line-break'> </span> a few times.  Not enough to<span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked in the tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped some.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a>.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them if they did not<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see me.  <a href='../subjects/8199' title='Elbert Lee Trinkle'>Trinkle</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was elected yester day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We are all sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> folks today.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> would of carried me to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> but I was a<span class='line-break'> </span> fraid there would be a<span class='line-break'> </span> cloud.  I am sorry that<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not go.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1342">
<h3><a name="page-1342">Thursday August  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in the tobacco</a> all day.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> killed two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and baked <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today is Mrs Cars birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  She is 67 years olde.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to the grove to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8183' title='revival meeting'>meeting</a>.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried her.  His mother &amp; aunt<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A <a href='../subjects/8200' title='Mr Roberson'>Mr Roberson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come here to see <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She wants to <a href='../subjects/8163' title='land sale'>sell her land</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie come home with the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a>.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I think she had<span class='line-break'> </span> a fine time to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Car <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> washed dishes for me.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1343">
<h3><a name="page-1343">Friday August  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some cloud<span class='line-break'> </span> about but no rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> going over the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> by<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Today they <a href='../subjects/8201' title='hauling rocks'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> rocks &amp; sand to work on<span class='line-break'> </span> the hearth in the dining<span class='line-break'> </span> room.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I done something all<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I to Whitefalls <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>to fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught several.<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna and Reese staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> most of the time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie put up six quarts<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> peeled the tomatoes.  That<span class='line-break'> </span> was a big help.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1344">
<h3><a name="page-1344">Saturday August  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a> all day<span class='line-break'> </span> and did not get near all<span class='line-break'> </span> done that they want to do.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8202' title='Mrs Butcher'>Mrs Butcher</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7464' title='Mrs Dalton'>Mrs Dalton</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  I was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to see them.  Mrs Butcher<span class='line-break'> </span> looks well and young for her.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I am glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Heard today that <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> is on his way home.<span class='line-break'> </span> He is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I am sorry for his<span class='line-break'> </span> mother and him.  Heard today<span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/8203' title='Rorner James'>Rorner James</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  There is several<span class='line-break'> </span> that dont care if he is <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie is lookin for <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to morrow.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1345">
<h3><a name="page-1345">Sunday August  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and a busy<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> and <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> was here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbard</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> three children and <a href='../subjects/8204' title='Mr Ran'>Mr Ran</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; wife come.  Mr Ran<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/8131' title='Rufus Boscombe Carr, Jr.'>Rufus Cars</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> Rufus come here with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad for them to<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> always glad for Mrs Car<span class='line-break'> </span> to stay with Josie.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> had a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a>.  I think <span class='line-break'> </span> all of them enjoyed them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1346">
<h3><a name="page-1346">Monday August  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A little rain this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> from here this mornin.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on the floor<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben went for <a href='../subjects/8205' title='cement'>cement</a><span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had a lot of company.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8206' title='Lettie'>Lettie</a> &amp; her children was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/7458' title='Mrs Anderson'>Mrs Anderson</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8207' title='Maud'>Maud</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a>, <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher</a> and <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Ernest Craddock</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim</a> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come by on their way<span class='line-break'> </span> home from the <a href='../subjects/8175' title='Red House, Virginia'>Red House</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georges</a> folks had plenty<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had a nice <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> ready.<span class='line-break'> </span> I don't know how many <span class='line-break'> </span> eat.  I had to come home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1347">
<h3><a name="page-1347">Tuesday August  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> finished puttin the floors in<span class='line-break'> </span> the basement.  They done<span class='line-break'> </span> a good job I think.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Dews</a> come here today for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> to help to cover the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a> that he lives in.  <a href='../subjects/8184' title='Walter Owen'>Walter<span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> was here today.  He is hunting<span class='line-break'> </span> a home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Josie and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> today.  Josie gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are the first that we<span class='line-break'> </span> have had.  The <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> dried up.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie made a lot of nice<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> yesterday.  That was<span class='line-break'> </span> all the <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a> that we<span class='line-break'> </span> have had to do anything<span class='line-break'> </span> with.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1348">
<h3><a name="page-1348">Wednesday August 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on a <a href='../subjects/8208' title='spring box'>spring box</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at the Owen <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a> half of<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Cars</a> place to help put on<span class='line-break'> </span> a roof.  Come home &amp; him<span class='line-break'> </span> and three of the children<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> house to a <a href='../subjects/7774' title='picture show'>picture show</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught several <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Was a crowd of people<span class='line-break'> </span> at Whitefalls on a <a href='../subjects/7934' title='picnic'>picknic</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would guess there was as<span class='line-break'> </span> many as 40 people.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There is a <a href='../subjects/8209' title='negro association'>negro assosiation</a><span class='line-break'> </span> going on at <a href='../subjects/7217' title='Glenland, Virginia'>Glendland</a>.  We met<span class='line-break'> </span> a lot going home.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> come by <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace B</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1349">
<h3><a name="page-1349">Thursday August 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some sand and put<span class='line-break'> </span> a round the <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a>.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> cut up the mulberrie tree.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry brought the <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> spent the day at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a>.  She had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped to put<span class='line-break'> </span> on the roof at <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Cars</a><span class='line-break'> </span> place and build a porch.<span class='line-break'> </span> I staid at home for<span class='line-break'> </span> one time with the children.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  Did not try to <span class='line-break'> </span> do any other work.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> was very good for<span class='line-break'> </span> her to be.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; family<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to see<span class='line-break'> </span> their new home.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1350">
<h3><a name="page-1350">Friday August 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> to work on a porch.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Powers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to spend the day.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went home today.  He left<span class='line-break'> </span> here walking.  Dont know<span class='line-break'> </span> how he made it.  Hope he got<span class='line-break'> </span> some way to ride.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  We made<span class='line-break'> </span> it fine.  I worked as<span class='line-break'> </span> little on we coud make<span class='line-break'> </span> out with.  Edna &amp; Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> helpe to cut some brush<span class='line-break'> </span> and drag it out of the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1351">
<h3><a name="page-1351">Saturday August 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I brought home 21 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all small.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> cooked them for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.  She made<span class='line-break'> </span> Edna a <a href='../subjects/8210' title='gown'>gown</a>.  Edna <span class='line-break'> </span> is very glad of it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> No rain yet.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> it so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I miss her if I<span class='line-break'> </span> dont see her often.<span class='line-break'> </span> I guess I will get use<span class='line-break'> </span> to not seeing her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1352">
<h3><a name="page-1352">Sunday August 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home all<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> as good as they could<span class='line-break'> </span> be.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> made a <a href='../subjects/8211' title='swing'>swing</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for the porch and put it <span class='line-break'> </span> up.  I think it is fine.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They had some<span class='line-break'> </span> mellons.  They were very fine<span class='line-break'> </span> in flavor.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie went to look<span class='line-break'> </span> for the <a href='../subjects/8059' title='turkeys'>turkeys</a>.  Did not find<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  I hope nothing wont<span class='line-break'> </span> happen to them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> come home ok tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> We were all so glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to see him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1353">
<h3><a name="page-1353">Monday August 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> worked in the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  Ben <a href='../subjects/8212' title='insecticide'>sprayed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some of his.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>cand</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.  Carried the <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/7841' title='spring'>spring</a> and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> the milk that was ready<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  Fixed the<span class='line-break'> </span> churn and churned.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carried some of the milk <span class='line-break'> </span> to the spring then dug<span class='line-break'> </span> bait.  That is a big job<span class='line-break'> </span> now.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried me<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> to White<span class='line-break'> </span> falls.  I caught a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Come by <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> bough two sacks of<span class='line-break'> </span> salt[?].  <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Otie Kellie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8213' title='Howard Strange'>Howard Strange</a> was at the store.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1354">
<h3><a name="page-1354">Tuesday August 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  A little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked <span class='line-break'> </span> in the tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and two colored men<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> place to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut some wood</a>.  It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and they come back early.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the little<span class='line-break'> </span> children come here<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; stayed with us.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese come for them with<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  I was glad that he come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I have staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home all day for one <span class='line-break'> </span> time.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1355">
<h3><a name="page-1355">Wednesday August 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little rain this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Clear this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>work in<span class='line-break'> </span> the tobacco</a> this morning.  Word<span class='line-break'> </span> came that <a href='../subjects/8214' title='Ursula Lewis'>Miss Ursal[?] Lewis</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was lost from the milkin place.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys from here and all over the<span class='line-break'> </span> neighborhood went to look for<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  They found her unharmed.<span class='line-break'> </span> She just went a way because<span class='line-break'> </span> she was mad.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> raked and<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a>.  I was afraid<span class='line-break'> </span> she would be <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Blair come here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was at <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They had a crowd this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/316' title='Mrs Kellie'>Mrs Kellie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8086' title='Jennie Owen'>Mrs</a> <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> and six<span class='line-break'> </span> children, <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> I.  They had plenty of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a>.  Two men<span class='line-break'> </span> was going <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>to speak</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1356">
<h3><a name="page-1356">Thursday August 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked<span class='line-break'> </span> in their tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made her a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this morning,<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8216' title='silk'>silk</a> that <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> gave her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we all went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  They had company.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them all.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>, <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> Fran[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8217' title='Charley Brumfield'>Charley Brumfield</a>. <a href='../subjects/7752' title='Lottie Kellie'>Lottie<span class='line-break'> </span> Kellie</a> &amp; two children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8218' title='Mr Kellie'>Mr Kellie</a> brought them<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; come for them.  He is<span class='line-break'> </span> good to take them around.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8219' title='Rorer'>Rorer</a> the <a href='../subjects/8220' title='commissioner'>commioner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come while we were there.<span class='line-break'> </span> He took the list of <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; I.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1357">
<h3><a name="page-1357">Friday August 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  The men<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked in the tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> They say that the <a href='../subjects/8221' title='hornworms'>worms</a> are<span class='line-break'> </span> very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> six <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>cans</a> of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>, &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Powers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/8222' title='Mrs Fletcher Carr'>Mrs Fletcher Car</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> children.  Ben said he did<span class='line-break'> </span> not get out of the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I know he did not stay long<span class='line-break'> </span> any where.  Tonight Ben &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has gone after them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I sent 8 <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8223' title='Miss Anna Hubbard'>Miss Anna Hubbard</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Have <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1358">
<h3><a name="page-1358">Saturday August 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked on their tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.  They helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> clear out his <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jose <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin let <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> me to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> went.  They <a href='../subjects/8164' title='swimming'>bathed</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a> and had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I caught 20 little<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  When I got home<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> was there.  She had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7646' title='Carey James Jefferson'>Ola's little boy</a> with her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad she come.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> have slept most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> time to night but I could<span class='line-break'> </span> not help it.  I had bin on<span class='line-break'> </span> my feet all day nearly.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Reese brought me home.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; the children<span class='line-break'> </span> come with me.  I thank them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1359">
<h3><a name="page-1359">Sunday August 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Oh how we<span class='line-break'> </span> need rain.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and little <a href='../subjects/7646' title='Carey James Jefferson'>Cary Jefferson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was with us today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> come for<span class='line-break'> </span> them tonight.  They have<span class='line-break'> </span> not bin gone but a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Hope that they<span class='line-break'> </span> will get home safe.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> &amp; her family<span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad<span class='line-break'> </span> for them to come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> when he was<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>cureing tobacco</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I know that Jim is<span class='line-break'> </span> lonesome some times.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmoth</a> today.  I know her<span class='line-break'> </span> mother will miss her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1360">
<h3><a name="page-1360">Monday August 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> dry day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to get the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> tire cut.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got <a href='../subjects/165' title='horseshoes'>horse shoes</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> put them on him self.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> have gone to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children are all here.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> have<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to sleep.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> up stairs reading.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has polished my shoes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that she did.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed some today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> cleaned the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a> some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to Strait Stone this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie got goods to make <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> blouses.  I was there this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  She was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a> on them.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1361">
<h3><a name="page-1361">Tuesday August 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled wood</a> to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They are thinking a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting tobacco</a> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7854' title='Worshams pond'>Worshams pond</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch anything</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had dinner with<span class='line-break'> </span> us and enjoyed it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wish I was close to<span class='line-break'> </span> the pond so I could go<span class='line-break'> </span> and not bother no one.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am willing to worke<span class='line-break'> </span> as much as I am able.<span class='line-break'> </span> That is a bout all that<span class='line-break'> </span> I ask them to take me<span class='line-break'> </span> and some times they wont<span class='line-break'> </span> do that.  I know that I give<span class='line-break'> </span> them here trouble.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1362">
<h3><a name="page-1362">Wednesday August 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> dry day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> helped<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>caned</a> three <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>cans</a> of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> this evening.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/8210' title='gown'>gown</a>.  Edna<span class='line-break'> </span> is proud of her new gowns.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> while.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She has done a lot of sewing<span class='line-break'> </span> for her children.  I dont<span class='line-break'> </span> see how she does as well<span class='line-break'> </span> as she does with so many<span class='line-break'> </span> to do for.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  He said<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce</a> was helping his <span class='line-break'> </span> mother <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> tomatoes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Some of them should<span class='line-break'> </span> her for she needs help.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> got in the <a href='../subjects/7363' title='corn field'>corn field</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Josie got him out.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1363">
<h3><a name="page-1363">Thursday August 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> dry day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> a cureing of tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> the most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  This evening she<span class='line-break'> </span> gathered some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and strung them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried me &amp; <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a>.  I think they had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good time batheing.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> come a<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  I caught several<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I peiced one block <span class='line-break'> </span> for my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1364">
<h3><a name="page-1364">Friday August 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> has worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day trying <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>get it to yellow</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7601' title='Fletcher Carr'>Fletcher Car</a> and family<span class='line-break'> </span> up here.  He has 6 children.<span class='line-break'> </span> We have not bin lonesome<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  This evening <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> come.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Carley[?] Harvey &amp; <a href='../subjects/8043' title='Virginia Moses'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Moses</a> was <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning at <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese<span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> carried <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> to Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and some others<span class='line-break'> </span> met at <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Richard Woodings</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut some tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for him.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am going to sleep in the<span class='line-break'> </span> hall to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1365">
<h3><a name="page-1365">Saturday August 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired his<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7601' title='Fletcher Carr'>Fletcher Car</a> most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> them to <a href='../subjects/7607' title='Mr Power'>Mr Powers</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to stay a while.  <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is hunting hair pins.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All of the rest of them<span class='line-break'> </span> have gone to bed.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1366">
<h3><a name="page-1366">Sunday August 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight and we need it so <span class='line-break'> </span> bad.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> staid <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
