<p> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a while this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Nellie and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and dressed[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> and started home.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried them to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I though that<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben was going to Gretna<span class='line-break'> </span> and that we would go with<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  He did not go and we<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> stopped in at <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr Hutchersons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has put<span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1367">
<h3><a name="page-1367">Monday August 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning but no rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a><span class='line-break'> </span> his all day and part <span class='line-break'> </span> of tonight.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> two baskets of <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> brought them to the house.<span class='line-break'> </span> I helped peel them.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>put up 24 quarts</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman<span class='line-break'> </span> Booker</a> sowed him a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip patch</a> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I cant get<span class='line-break'> </span> use to the idie that Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> is going to come there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I most shurely hate<span class='line-break'> </span> to think that Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> is going to <span class='line-break'> </span> leave.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1368">
<h3><a name="page-1368">Tuesday August 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good hot day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> then they<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  All you hear a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> it is how sorry it is.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and then got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We both have<span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went and picked<span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner tomorrow.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1369">
<h3><a name="page-1369">Wednesday August 31, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  No rain<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> help.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a>.  Otho cut tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Josie walked to <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs.  Ben met her<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and brough<span class='line-break'> </span> her home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin very good today.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked 47 button<span class='line-break'> </span> holes in some clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> little girls.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma Owen</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8227' title='Fannie Brumfield'>Fannie Brumfield</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1370">
<h3><a name="page-1370">Thursday September  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>, <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>, <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a>, <a href='../subjects/7656' title='Paul'>Paul</a>, <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>a show</a>.  I think they<span class='line-break'> </span> all enjoyed it very much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today is <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smiths</a><span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  He is nine years<span class='line-break'> </span> olde.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> makeing Roy some <a href='../subjects/7892' title='blouses'>blouses</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am going to make the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I put my <a href='../subjects/7987' title='glasses'>glasses</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>range</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and ruined them.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> have mised them so<span class='line-break'> </span> much today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1371">
<h3><a name="page-1371">Friday September  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  Ben will work<span class='line-break'> </span> on his all night.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> is <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>proffessor</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/8228' title='Renan School'>Renan School</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> here toay.  I did not see<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Reese carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  The boys <a href='../subjects/8164' title='swimming'>bathed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught 31 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy Smith</a> carried 4<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8221' title='hornworms'>horn worms</a> to see if the<span class='line-break'> </span> fish would bite them.  (They<span class='line-break'> </span> would.)</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1372">
<h3><a name="page-1372">Saturday September  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A hot dry day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired<span class='line-break'> </span> on his tobacco</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> while Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Ben brought<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> home from<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.  <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/8122' title='Irvin Lewis Mother'>his mother</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a> and <a href='../subjects/7650' title='Aubrey Brumfield'>Aubra Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8229' title='Ralph East'>Ralph East</a> to White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  We caught several<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/8230' title='Jim Thomson'>Jim Thomson</a> was there<span class='line-break'> </span> with his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  He brought<span class='line-break'> </span> us part the way home<span class='line-break'> </span> and I was glad that he did.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1373">
<h3><a name="page-1373">Sunday September  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day most of the<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Had a little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am so glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> what it did.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> and <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried<span class='line-break'> </span> chicken</a> and plenty <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>, <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and Josie went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got home at sun<span class='line-break'> </span> down.  Josie made <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and we had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  To night Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Have not come home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Josie met <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> on his way<span class='line-break'> </span> home from <a href='../subjects/8231' title='Georgia'>Georgie</a>.  I<span class='line-break'> </span> know they will be glad to see him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1374">
<h3><a name="page-1374">Monday September  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  They cut Jims<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco and commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Bens</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> a pair of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie Brumfield</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma Owen</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynols</a> com to<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins and <a href='../subjects/8164' title='swimming'>bathed</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the pond that the children<span class='line-break'> </span> has in the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/8078' title='heifer'>heifer</a> got hurt<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> very sorry it happened.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1375">
<h3><a name="page-1375">Tuesday September  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Another hot dry day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting his<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> and finished Jims.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a>.  Made <a href='../subjects/9095' title='waist'>waists</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got what <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> we<span class='line-break'> </span> had.  This evening I <span class='line-break'> </span> worked <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Pauls</a> waists.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I and the<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewing</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> has done more sewing<span class='line-break'> </span> than any one that I <span class='line-break'> </span> know of.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I want to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> I intend to go to see her<span class='line-break'> </span> soon if I can get to any<span class='line-break'> </span> way.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1376">
<h3><a name="page-1376">Wednesday September  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  No rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> The boys helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I<span class='line-break'> </span> washed this morning.  Finished <span class='line-break'> </span> in time to get a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Josie made two <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the least time I ever<span class='line-break'> </span> thought of.  We had <a href='../subjects/7954' title='salmon'>salmon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8233' title='canned beef'>canned beef</a>.  All could be<span class='line-break'> </span> got ready quick.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I worked on <a href='../subjects/91' title='button holes'>button holes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a pair<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/8234' title='bloomers'>bloomers</a> and picked<span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Edna &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> pulled<span class='line-break'> </span> pea vines and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> through the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; climed the cyckamore<span class='line-break'> </span> tree.  They ask me to write<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout as I did not know<span class='line-break'> </span> any thing to write.  I did it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1377">
<h3><a name="page-1377">Thursday September  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Another hot day.<span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks helped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> finish <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I caught several <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had a good evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> said she was glad<span class='line-break'> </span> to have him with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> the most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry that we cant<span class='line-break'> </span> get any help.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> getting olde and cant do<span class='line-break'> </span> very much and dont<span class='line-break'> </span> do what I might.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> sonigh a sleep that I<span class='line-break'> </span> cant hardly write.  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1378">
<h3><a name="page-1378">Friday September  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  We were so<span class='line-break'> </span> glad of what did fall.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I worked some button <span class='line-break'> </span> holes.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> will<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>stay at the barn</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a> to night a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come by the pea<span class='line-break'> </span> patch.  There is a lot <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> dry and need <span class='line-break'> </span> to be gathered.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Marvin went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8235' title='Mrs Kates'>Mrs Kates</a> place this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening and got a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.  Fruit is hard <span class='line-break'> </span> to find a bout here<span class='line-break'> </span> this year.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1379">
<h3><a name="page-1379">Saturday September 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>worked on their tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> fireing it</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I picked some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> this morning.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I to the<span class='line-break'> </span> river.  He did not want<span class='line-break'> </span> to go but went.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch</a> any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing much.  We stoped<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there and <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She had fried <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  We did enjoy<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  She <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> on <span class='line-break'> </span> the men folks clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Dodson Bailis</a> come to see Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1380">
<h3><a name="page-1380">Sunday September 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until after twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired on his tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  This evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynols</a>.  They had<span class='line-break'> </span> a house full of company.  <span class='line-break'> </span> All their people.  <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> family, <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack</a> &amp; family and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8230' title='Jim Thomson'>Jim Thomson</a> &amp; family and<span class='line-break'> </span> I.  I think they enjoyed having<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  They made <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and had <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Rubin</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me home on <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thomsons</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a> &amp; children.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they went.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> want to go soon to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them all.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>good rain</a> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles</a> &amp; wife come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1381">
<h3><a name="page-1381">Monday September 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7923' title='hauling corn'>hauled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to pick <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> was not satisfied<span class='line-break'> </span> so Josie had to quit and<span class='line-break'> </span> bring Mabel home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> picked what I could.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> picked some this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8237' title='Nettie Hendrickes'>Nettie Hendrickes</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/7885' title='Alice Hubbard'>Miss Alice Hubbard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> School at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> commenced<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I do hope that we<span class='line-break'> </span> can have a good <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this time.  Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7907' title='possum hunting'>possum hunting</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1382">
<h3><a name="page-1382">Tuesday September 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> after he got the engine<span class='line-break'> </span> to work.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> &amp; I washed.  Josie used<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8127' title='washing machine'>machine</a> part of the time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was at work<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roys</a> <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a>'s <a href='../subjects/8264' title='possum'>possum</a> got out of<span class='line-break'> </span> the box that is a [pen mark]  He <span class='line-break'> </span> was gone this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> keeps fretting.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> a fraid she is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1383">
<h3><a name="page-1383">Wednesday September 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> the land that they want to<span class='line-break'> </span> sow in grain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7923' title='hauling corn'>hauled<span class='line-break'> </span> some wood</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They got <a href='../subjects/7977' title='books'>books</a> for the children<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8238' title='cloth'>cloth</a> to make them<span class='line-break'> </span> clothes.  Josie <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  I have bin<span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day today.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> the little girls come<span class='line-break'> </span> down here and staid<span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad that they come.<span class='line-break'> </span> We need rain a gain<span class='line-break'> </span> very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>huntting</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1384">
<h3><a name="page-1384">Thursday September 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a little rain<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout day this morning.  Need<span class='line-break'> </span> more bad.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this morning.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carried corn &amp; rye &amp; <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with him on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> while they<span class='line-break'> </span> ground the grain.  I caught<span class='line-break'> </span> several <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  I intend to fry<span class='line-break'> </span> them in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has raked a place<span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> and sowed<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> on it.  I do hope<span class='line-break'> </span> that they may come up and<span class='line-break'> </span> grow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie dug bait for <span class='line-break'> </span> me while I changed my <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> and <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1385">
<h3><a name="page-1385">Friday September 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7390' title='Smith'>Smith</a> carried him.  All<span class='line-break'> </span> the Smith children<span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was up there &amp; come<span class='line-break'> </span> with them home.  The<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a> boys went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham to day to enter<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> drove<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  He ran over<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a>.  Dont know <span class='line-break'> </span> how bad it was hurt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> &amp; Mollie was at<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins to day.  Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> come down here.  Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> stay but a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> is in <a href='../subjects/8239' title='Spray, North Carolina'>NC<span class='line-break'> </span> at Spray</a>.  She claims to be<span class='line-break'> </span> visiting <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen Brumfield</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1386">
<h3><a name="page-1386">Saturday September 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Was <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning but <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>cleared off</a> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> jobed a round all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut some corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I washed<span class='line-break'> </span> a little.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> to <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owens</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning to have her lip<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on.  I am troubled<span class='line-break'> </span> a bout her.  Hope she may<span class='line-break'> </span> soon be <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried me to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  I caught a<span class='line-break'> </span> few <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1387">
<h3><a name="page-1387">Sunday September 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid here all night last night.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home most<span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  Went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> had company.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>Mr John Smith</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8241' title='Gallie Burger'>Gallie Burger</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  All of the<span class='line-break'> </span> children and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield went.  <a href='../subjects/8242' title='Mr Hargrave'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Hargrave</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1388">
<h3><a name="page-1388">Monday September 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> dry day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and his<span class='line-break'> </span> hand helped them this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was no one at the<span class='line-break'> </span> store.  The children went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come home very much <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a>.  I hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> will soon be <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I washed some<span class='line-break'> </span> quilts this morning.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> so glad that we are done<span class='line-break'> </span> that job.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie spent the evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mending</a> on the clothes.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Some of <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> children<span class='line-break'> </span> has bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some on a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and to night.  Every one has<span class='line-break'> </span> gone to bed and I will go <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1389">
<h3><a name="page-1389">Tuesday September 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> tonight.  We need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain very bad.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cutting corn</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I wanted to<span class='line-break'> </span> help her but did not do much.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> was so cross and did<span class='line-break'> </span> not want to stay at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7624' title='wash house'>wash house</a>.  I come to the house<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  Josie helped<span class='line-break'> </span> get <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on<span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> all evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She said <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was shelling<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> and she helped<span class='line-break'> </span> her while she was there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/8243' title='tobacco markets'>tobacco markets</a> opened to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  We heard that the tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> very low.  I was in hopes<span class='line-break'> </span> that good would sell well.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; Jim has not got any good.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1390">
<h3><a name="page-1390">Wednesday September 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  It is raining now.<span class='line-break'> </span> That is what we need.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Mr Eanes</a>'s<span class='line-break'> </span> today to help cover a <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and got<span class='line-break'> </span> out <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  Fixin to go to<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> starched her clothes<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> late this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was shelling<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a>.  I shelled <span class='line-break'> </span> while I staid.  Come home <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.  By the <span class='line-break'> </span> time a done that Josie had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> ready.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Jim went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a>.  I guess they<span class='line-break'> </span> will get wet comeing home.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1391">
<h3><a name="page-1391">Thursday September 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> last night and<span class='line-break'> </span> every one is so glad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Had his <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cleaned and some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a><span class='line-break'> </span> ground.  He <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowing</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnips</a> and worked on<span class='line-break'> </span> the trees triming them up.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked at <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Eanes's</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I will be glad when he gets <span class='line-break'> </span> done there.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was shelling<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  Josie helped her<span class='line-break'> </span> while she was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Well I am a sleep.  Will quit<span class='line-break'> </span> now.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1392">
<h3><a name="page-1392">Friday September 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked at <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Eanes's</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed the dineing<span class='line-break'> </span> room floor &amp; hall steps.<span class='line-break'> </span> Cleane up all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> &amp; and killed<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and cooked it<span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Josie baked<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> come a while. <span class='line-break'> </span> I walked with her as<span class='line-break'> </span> far as <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  The boys<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to Marvins to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> has bin haveing <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>toothache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorrie for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I peiced on my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Had thought to finish it<span class='line-break'> </span> this week but I know<span class='line-break'> </span> now that I will not finish<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  Today is <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smiths</a> birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1393">
<h3><a name="page-1393">Saturday September 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Eanes</a> to work.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben come home and went<span class='line-break'> </span> for the teacers.  <a href='../subjects/8245' title='Miss Ferguson'>Miss Fergerson</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8246' title='Miss Treer'>Miss Treer</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The proffesor did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> come this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I am glad that <span class='line-break'> </span> he come.  Ben carried the<span class='line-break'> </span> ladies home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  Josie cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to John <span class='line-break'> </span> Smiths this evening.  Carried<span class='line-break'> </span> all the children.  I went<span class='line-break'> </span> as far as <a href='../subjects/7328' title='Mr Johnson'>Mr Johnsons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> bought four <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>Mr John Smith</a>.  Hope he<span class='line-break'> </span> may have good luck with<span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1394">
<h3><a name="page-1394">Sunday September 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a sprinkle of <span class='line-break'> </span> rain this morning.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin here all day.  Will stay<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/361' title='mountain'>mountain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning to hunt <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Did not find many.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> We eat late and did not<span class='line-break'> </span> get any <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Some one gave his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/986' title='dog'>dog</a> a dose this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and she <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> thought a heap of her.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would like to know<span class='line-break'> </span> who did it but never<span class='line-break'> </span> will I dont expect.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1395">
<h3><a name="page-1395">Monday September 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day &amp; <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> no to<span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seeds</a>.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to a <a href='../subjects/8041' title='farmers meeting'>farmers meeting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He joined <a href='../subjects/8072' title='Farmers Union'>the unioin</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was a big crowd<span class='line-break'> </span> so Ben said.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim is helping <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> tonight.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> has gone <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  We went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin sewin on a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1396">
<h3><a name="page-1396">Tuesday September 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  A little rain.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> tinkered a round<span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> and Cedar<span class='line-break'> </span> Forest.  Josie bought a set of<span class='line-break'> </span> cups and saucers.  Paid $1.50<span class='line-break'> </span> for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie made <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> two<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirts</a> today.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on<span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  I pulled some<span class='line-break'> </span> grass from among the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries vines</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We have heard that Emmet<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield has <a href='../subjects/8248' title='whooping cough'>whooping<span class='line-break'> </span> cough</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1397">
<h3><a name="page-1397">Wednesday September 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Eanes's</a> to finish the <span class='line-break'> </span> job of tining his house.<span class='line-break'> </span> Come home at twelve.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> all the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening they <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> log to carry to the saw<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>mill</a>.  To night <a href='../subjects/8642' title='Mr Fretwell'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Fretwell</a> is here to spend<span class='line-break'> </span> the night.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/8075' title='sowing grass'>sowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some.  She has bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth ache</a> some<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was very much<span class='line-break'> </span> complaining.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This written Thursday morning<span class='line-break'> </span> at five oclock.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1398">
<h3><a name="page-1398">Thursday September 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a><span class='line-break'> </span> twice.  Carried two logs &amp; brought<span class='line-break'> </span> back <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come and spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her.  A <a href='../subjects/8250' title='photographer'>picture agent</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come here to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/217' title='agents'>Agents</a> is plentyful now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I walked with<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate as far as <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin was <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> broke a chamber <span class='line-break'> </span> vessel and let <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fall</a> off the bed then had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good cry and went <span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim and Ben helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I carried <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a><span class='line-break'> </span> home this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1399">
<h3><a name="page-1399">Friday September 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain here.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved some tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carried two logs one this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning and one this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this  morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> ironed this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  Did not catch<span class='line-break'> </span> many <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a><span class='line-break'> </span> stuck a nail in his foot<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I hope it wont<span class='line-break'> </span> hurt him long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Reese &amp; I stoped at <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mt<span class='line-break'> </span> Airy</a> and at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> bought a few things at <span class='line-break'> </span> both places.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1400">
<h3><a name="page-1400">Saturday October  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> and dry.<span class='line-break'> </span> We need rain very bad.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/8244' title='Mr Eanes'>Eanes</a> a gain<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  They eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> planted a <span class='line-break'> </span> gate post and done a round<span class='line-break'> </span> here all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Worked all the evening <span class='line-break'> </span> at one thing an other.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> a few things<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berry vines</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a little getting the grass out.<span class='line-break'> </span> We bought a peice of<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> this morning.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> all enjoyed it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today was <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabels</a> birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  She has had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> day for her.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> gathered<span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1401">
<h3><a name="page-1401">Sunday October  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at home until after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> then I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols</a>.  They were eating <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a>, <a href='../subjects/8251' title='Mr Keef'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Keef</a> and <a href='../subjects/7831' title='Mr Hankins'>Mr Hankins</a>,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8230' title='Jim Thomson'>Jim Thomson</a> &amp; family,<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie Reynols</a> and family.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; the<span class='line-break'> </span> children went to Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Thomsons then come to<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynols.  They brought me<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid home all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went by <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were all up and <span class='line-break'> </span> a bought.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1402">
<h3><a name="page-1402">Monday October  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a gain this evening.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped some tobacco</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has had the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth<span class='line-break'> </span> ache</a> all day.  She made<span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/70' title='apron'>three aprons</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  The children<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  We went <span class='line-break'> </span> for things that we had <span class='line-break'> </span> to have to live on.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had a good trip.<span class='line-break'> </span> It rained while we<span class='line-break'> </span> were at Gretna.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  He was<span class='line-break'> </span> working on his <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think it will be very <span class='line-break'> </span> nice when he gets it<span class='line-break'> </span> complete.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1403">
<h3><a name="page-1403">Tuesday October  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> a log and<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw<span class='line-break'> </span> mill</a>.  He brought <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a><span class='line-break'> </span> back when he come.  Jim and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/8253' title='Mr Cothron'>Mr Cothron</a>[?]<span class='line-break'> </span> come to see <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  He wanted her<span class='line-break'> </span> dues on the church.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I was starting<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  They carried<span class='line-break'> </span> us on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> that far.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad of the ride<span class='line-break'> </span> as Josie would had<span class='line-break'> </span> to carrie <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> all<span class='line-break'> </span> the way.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1404">
<h3><a name="page-1404">Wednesday October  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> helped them.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Booker</a> and a hand <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> on his place.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed all by<span class='line-break'> </span> her self today.  I staid<span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1405">
<h3><a name="page-1405">Thursday October  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on their <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> land.  <a href='../subjects/8169' title='Norman Booker'>Norman Booker</a><span class='line-break'> </span> had the <a href='../subjects/8255' title='drill'>drill</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed some wheat</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/8140' title='Mr Young'>Mr Young</a><span class='line-break'> </span> about <a href='../subjects/8258' title='electric generator'>the engine</a>.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> cant start it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
