<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> We straitened up in<span class='line-break'> </span> the lock room this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla Blair</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening and<span class='line-break'> </span> staid a little while.<span class='line-break'> </span> She wanted a <a href='../subjects/8256' title='breast pump'>breast<span class='line-break'> </span> pump</a> for <a href='../subjects/8257' title='Nettie Hendries'>Nettie Hendries</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went home with Isla.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them all.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1406">
<h3><a name="page-1406">Friday October  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> made some boxes to put<span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>spring branch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Jim went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.  Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  She scrubed<span class='line-break'> </span> the floor this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> washed this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben started <a href='../subjects/8258' title='electric generator'>the engine</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  We were all glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that he got it started.<span class='line-break'> </span> We used the <a href='../subjects/224' title='lamps'>lamps</a> last<span class='line-break'> </span> night and made out fine.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1407">
<h3><a name="page-1407">Saturday October  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning.  Soon <span class='line-break'> </span> cleared up and the <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a><span class='line-break'> </span> blowed the rest of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> and it is <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Guess there will be <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8259' title='Pearl Wigginton'>Pearl<span class='line-break'> </span> Wiginton</a> come to see us a<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> them home.  He was going to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> if they had not come.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols's</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She never will for get them.<span class='line-break'> </span> They were kind to her when she<span class='line-break'> </span> was in the hospital.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie, <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night to <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> or something<span class='line-break'> </span> of the sort.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Come home colde.  I staid <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1408">
<h3><a name="page-1408">Sunday October  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A cool day.  Some frost<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Powers.  They come home<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben went to meet<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim at Gretna.  They got<span class='line-break'> </span> home at dark.  I got supper<span class='line-break'> </span> at twelve.  Thought Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> and the rest of them would<span class='line-break'> </span> come home for dinner and<span class='line-break'> </span> they did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese sprained his arm<span class='line-break'> </span> trying to crank their car.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1409">
<h3><a name="page-1409">Monday October 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Windy and <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the <span class='line-break'> </span> island</a> for <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> offered to take me.<span class='line-break'> </span> I would of went but I had<span class='line-break'> </span> no one to stay with me at<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a>.  I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8260' title='Tom Wooding'>Mr Tom Woodings</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Found them able<span class='line-break'> </span> to get a bout.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> finished<span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/70' title='apron'>apron</a> for me this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I went to sleep<span class='line-break'> </span> while I am trying to<span class='line-break'> </span> write.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1410">
<h3><a name="page-1410">Tuesday October 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> put up the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> sweet and irish.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> tonight.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> have gone to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> for grass<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> has <a href='../subjects/8261' title='Julia Smith'>a girl</a> born<span class='line-break'> </span> this morning at two oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come over here this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed</a> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  To day is<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a> birth day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> here a little while tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  He traded<span class='line-break'> </span> some chickens.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got up the <a href='../subjects/7226' title='peanuts'>pea nuts</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1411">
<h3><a name="page-1411">Wednesday October 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> filled up <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It was very hard job.<span class='line-break'> </span> The land is so dry.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a> and <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> come to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <a href='../subjects/8261' title='Julia Smith'>and baby</a>.  Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and the children come<span class='line-break'> </span> home while I was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin had bin to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I think there will be <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1412">
<h3><a name="page-1412">Thursday October 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing frost</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowing</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked some corn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I washed some.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/46' title='pudding'>pudding</a>.  We all enjoyed <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie, <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> They all seemed to be<span class='line-break'> </span> getting on <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <a href='../subjects/8262' title='corn stalks'>corn<span class='line-break'> </span> stalks</a> today.  Every thing has<span class='line-break'> </span> dried up in the <a href='../subjects/321' title='pasture'>pasture</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> It is a gloomy time a bout<span class='line-break'> </span> something to feed on.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1413">
<h3><a name="page-1413">Friday October 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  There was a<span class='line-break'> </span> big <a href='../subjects/7544' title='frost'>frost</a> this morning.  Oh <span class='line-break'> </span> we need rain so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> a log<span class='line-break'> </span> to take to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw <span class='line-break'> </span> mill</a> in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> They went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Harveys this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed some wheat</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for her.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> most all day.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8088' title='Lucy Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynols</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> while we were there.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1414">
<h3><a name="page-1414">Saturday October 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Partly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/7533' title='hauling logs'>hauled logs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I got<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>, <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/8264' title='possum'>possomes</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>, <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and fixed<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  Did not<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing <a href='../subjects/7498' title='speaking'>to speak</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of.  We had good luck going<span class='line-break'> </span> and comeing.  Reese did not<span class='line-break'> </span> have any trouble with the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> come to spend <span class='line-break'> </span> the night with us.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she came.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1415">
<h3><a name="page-1415">Sunday October 16, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all was<span class='line-break'> </span> at home today.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett was here all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> and Alma has started<span class='line-break'> </span> home now ten o'clock at<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to her<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack Hubbard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; family was to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> No sign of rain yet.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1416">
<h3><a name="page-1416">Monday October 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  No sign of<span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved<span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7767' title='Chalk Level, Virginia'>Chalk Level</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to get some peices <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to make a <a href='../subjects/8265' title='roller'>roller</a> to roll<span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the roller all<span class='line-break'> </span> evening and did not finish<span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some on a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They are getting<span class='line-break'> </span> on very well there.  Tonight<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin &amp; Ben has gone<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunting</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/8266' title='Taz Wooding'>Mr Taz Wooding</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a><span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  Will be <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1417">
<h3><a name="page-1417">Tuesday October 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> worked on a <a href='../subjects/8265' title='roller'>roller</a> until<span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie had <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>three teeth pulled</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> She come home <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  Has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin inbed ever since.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope she may be better by<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/8266' title='Taz Wooding'>Mr Taz Woodings</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a> this evening.  I kept<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> this evening.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> was very good for her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Come home<span class='line-break'> </span> with their Dady when<span class='line-break'> </span> he come from Altavista.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1418">
<h3><a name="page-1418">Wednesday October 19, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> rolled his<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> bin up most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span> but is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>feeling bad</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> her teeth being pulled.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/8267' title='Martha Miller'>Martha Miller</a> made some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7477' title='soap'>soap</a> for us today.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> were glad to get her<span class='line-break'> </span> to make it.  <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> and <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a><span class='line-break'> </span> stayed here while Martha <span class='line-break'> </span> was makeing soap.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Dodson<span class='line-break'> </span> Bailiss</a> had to carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> one of his children<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/7799' title='hospital'>hospitle</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben went to the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> tonight to strip<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1419">
<h3><a name="page-1419">Thursday October 20, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped some <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this morning.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening they killed a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that we called <a href='../subjects/8268' title='Billy Sunday'>Billie<span class='line-break'> </span> Sunday</a>.  We had a wind<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a> last night and a<span class='line-break'> </span> little rain.  Not enough to <span class='line-break'> </span> do any good.  We need rain<span class='line-break'> </span> as bad as I ever have seen<span class='line-break'> </span> I think.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin bad off all day<span class='line-break'> </span> with her jaws and throat.<span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope she may be better<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.  She made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a negro<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7517' title='doll'>doll</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denias</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> Found them all <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Hope she is getting on<span class='line-break'> </span> ok.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1420">
<h3><a name="page-1420">Friday October 21, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped some tobacco</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/8269' title='Alcie Callands'>Alcie Callan</a> (col)<span class='line-break'> </span> washed for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  Kate <span class='line-break'> </span> got a peice of <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> walked and carried it home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I was very sorrie for her but<span class='line-break'> </span> could not help her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little<span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a>.  I do<span class='line-break'> </span> hope she will feel better soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie is very bad off with<span class='line-break'> </span> her jaws where she had<span class='line-break'> </span> her teeth pulled.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> they will get <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> has bin very good<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  The children all gave<span class='line-break'> </span> me a <a href='../subjects/7633' title='presents'>present</a> for my birthday.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> got a <a href='../subjects/7696' title='postcard'>card</a> from <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1421">
<h3><a name="page-1421">Saturday October 22, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bright day.  Not a cloud in<span class='line-break'> </span> sight.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is<span class='line-break'> </span> very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> with her<span class='line-break'> </span> jaw.  I know she suffers with it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.  Henry drove the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>team</a><span class='line-break'> </span> as far as <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mount Airy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> me to White Fall on <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>Bens car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch</a> any <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> did not get his grain ground.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went by <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was looking better than she did yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope that Josie &amp; Carrie may be <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well my birth day has bin a disapointment.<span class='line-break'> </span> I had hoped to catch some fish and<span class='line-break'> </span> I think Josie felt so bad that she<span class='line-break'> </span> freted with me all day.  Reese gave<span class='line-break'> </span> me a little sack of <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> for my birthday.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> and <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia</a> is here.<span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> to night.  I am so sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span> I hope to see some more birth days<span class='line-break'> </span> but I may not.  I am 75.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1422">
<h3><a name="page-1422">Sunday October 23, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> day &amp; dry day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We staid at home until<span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> to take <a href='../subjects/8267' title='Martha Miller'>Martha<span class='line-break'> </span> Miller</a> home.  They got back <span class='line-break'> </span> early in the evening.  Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> went without his dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin suffering with<span class='line-break'> </span> her jaw all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; her<span class='line-break'> </span> went to see the <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>doctor</a><span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  He <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>worked<span class='line-break'> </span> on it some</a> and she is feeling<span class='line-break'> </span> some better to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia Brumfield</a> has bin<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>Eva</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1423">
<h3><a name="page-1423">Monday October 24, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to help <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> get ready to sow <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> has bin very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> We had the <a href='../subjects/293' title='doctor'>doctor</a> to see<span class='line-break'> </span> her this morning.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home.  Him and <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a><span class='line-break'> </span> played out of the doors most<span class='line-break'> </span> of day.  I got a nice box of <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> sent it.  I have not eat any<span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  I have not bin to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> was to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> to day.  I am glad<span class='line-break'> </span> that she come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Christenia</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went from here this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> I put out ten little <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a><span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1424">
<h3><a name="page-1424">Tuesday October 25, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> day.  Not a cloud<span class='line-break'> </span> in sight.  The <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> is blowing<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> did not.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin bad<span class='line-break'> </span> off all day.  She is not suffering<span class='line-break'> </span> so bad tonight.  I hope she will<span class='line-break'> </span> soon be up a gain.  <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to see her today.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> went for <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> She was gone to <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a>.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> has gone there after her.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> have not got here yet.  I am<span class='line-break'> </span> sorry that the wind is blowing<span class='line-break'> </span> so hard.  I have not bin to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this week.  Hope Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> may be <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a> enough that I<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> go soon.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> has bin good for her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I started <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Would be glad to hear from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a> folks.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1425">
<h3><a name="page-1425">Wednesday October 26, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A partly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to sow <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> staid<span class='line-break'> </span> here.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella</a><span class='line-break'> </span> got here last night about<span class='line-break'> </span> ten.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> is much better<span class='line-break'> </span> off to night.  Ben carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/286' title='Mrs. Oley Hubbard'>Mrs Hubbard</a> home this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come a while &amp; <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come a while.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> walked a way togather.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few<span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is looking bad.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1426">
<h3><a name="page-1426">Thursday October 27, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Somewhat <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to help <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> finish <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowing wheat</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> got done and he got<span class='line-break'> </span> home a bout dark.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  They are at<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> now <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tying tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin up all day.<span class='line-break'> </span> Helped to got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was there.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> enjoyed my visit very much.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ren come to the house.  He was<span class='line-break'> </span> very friendly.  They Ren &amp; and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> are <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a> fixed for a <span class='line-break'> </span> liveing and have a nice<span class='line-break'> </span> family of children.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> for them to do well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I walked to Rens.  Am afraid<span class='line-break'> </span> I wont be able to do that <span class='line-break'> </span> long.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1427">
<h3><a name="page-1427">Friday October 28, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning but no rain and we need<span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> &amp; went to the <a href='../subjects/8272' title='grist mill'>mill</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> He got his grain ground.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I done all of the <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feeding</a><span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> &amp; <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8273' title='possums'>opossomes</a>.  Helped get <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> entertainment.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8269' title='Alcie Callands'>Alcie Callands</a> washed for<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie today.  She is a good<span class='line-break'> </span> hand.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim &amp; Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mayhews</a> for a <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hog</a> that Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> bought from Mayhew.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I hope he may have good luck <span class='line-break'> </span> with her.  There was to be<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8193' title='lecture'>speaking</a> at the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Our folks did not go.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1428">
<h3><a name="page-1428">Saturday October 29, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> most of the day.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the island</a><span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/8274' title='roofing'>roofing</a>.  I went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> We did not stay long.  We come<span class='line-break'> </span> home and eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> all except Jim went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to a Halowene<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a>.  They solde <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  There was a big crowd<span class='line-break'> </span> and I think they nearly all<span class='line-break'> </span> had a good time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was 4 of my chiildren<span class='line-break'> </span> and a lot of my grand<span class='line-break'> </span> children &amp; great grand<span class='line-break'> </span> children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to sleep and <span class='line-break'> </span> let the <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a> get on my<span class='line-break'> </span> book.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1429">
<h3><a name="page-1429">Sunday October 30, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The firs day<span class='line-break'> </span> that it has <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> for a<span class='line-break'> </span> long time.  I am glad it has<span class='line-break'> </span> rained for we needed it so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home to day<span class='line-break'> </span> except I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  They were all<span class='line-break'> </span> getting on well.  There was<span class='line-break'> </span> to be <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> at Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone.  Marvin went to meet<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/8275' title='professor'>professor</a> and they were<span class='line-break'> </span> going togather.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was with us to day.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> am glad to have her any<span class='line-break'> </span> time she will come.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1430">
<h3><a name="page-1430">Monday October 31, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  The land is good<span class='line-break'> </span> and wet the first time in<span class='line-break'> </span> about five months.  I hope<span class='line-break'> </span> it will quit raining for this<span class='line-break'> </span> time soon.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to meet some<span class='line-break'> </span> one.  A <a href='../subjects/8276' title='Mr Shelton'>Mr Shelton</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> with him.  I know that they<span class='line-break'> </span> had a rough time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie</a> is there with her<span class='line-break'> </span> two little children &amp; <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Net</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with one.  They are good looking<span class='line-break'> </span> children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to bed<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I hope he may be well<span class='line-break'> </span> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a><span class='line-break'> </span> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1431">
<h3><a name="page-1431">Tuesday November  1, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  No rain today.<span class='line-break'> </span> The land is good we for the<span class='line-break'> </span> first time in a bout five months.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The boys <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> finished a <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>cureing</a> for <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a><span class='line-break'> </span> all day of <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with<span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  It <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> very <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> The children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I killed and dressed an<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8273' title='possums'>opossome</a>.  The first one that<span class='line-break'> </span> I ever killed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped move a cureing<span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  We sent to <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> and got two pounds<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  Paid <a href='../subjects/7482' title='money'>35 cts</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> pound.  That is the first that<span class='line-break'> </span> we have bought this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This writing was done at<span class='line-break'> </span> three oclock Nov the 2nd.  I forgot<span class='line-break'> </span> to write last night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1432">
<h3><a name="page-1432">Wednesday November  2, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>with tobacco</a>.  Solde well for<span class='line-break'> </span> what it was.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna today with tobacco.  Did<span class='line-break'> </span> not <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>sell</a> so well.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> worked<span class='line-break'> </span> all day fixin for company.<span class='line-break'> </span> She cooked a <a href='../subjects/8273' title='possums'>posome</a> for<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Anderson</a> <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I think they had a nice wedding.<span class='line-break'> </span> Gorden &amp; Lizzie and <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come by here for me &amp; brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me home.  I certainly did thank<span class='line-break'> </span> them for the rememberance.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7262' title='Charlottesville, Virginia'>Charlotsville</a><span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and had a <a href='../subjects/8277' title='warts'>wart</a><span class='line-break'> </span> cut off of her mouth.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/8093' title='Melissa Mayhew'>wife</a> come and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> supper with us.  <a href='../subjects/8278' title='Mr Gambol'>Mr Gambol</a><span class='line-break'> </span> eat supper with us.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1433">
<h3><a name="page-1433">Thursday November  3, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  No rain.  <a href='../subjects/8278' title='Mr Gambol'>Mr Gambol</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> from here this morning.  John<span class='line-break'> </span> carried the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>team</a> and <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7502' title='Edwin Brumfield'>Edwin</a> brought them home<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> killed<span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> this morning.  Jim killed<span class='line-break'> </span> an <a href='../subjects/8273' title='possums'>opossome</a> this evening.  He<span class='line-break'> </span> intends to take it to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a><span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  She went to <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this evening to see <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> and they had both<span class='line-break'> </span> gone home.  She had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> visit any way.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes this<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> staid with<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1434">
<h3><a name="page-1434">Friday November  4, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried him.  He carried<span class='line-break'> </span> several things.  I went with him.<span class='line-break'> </span> We got home a little after dark.<span class='line-break'> </span> I did not go in a store.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> did not have time.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> Today is <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> birth<span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I have thought of many<span class='line-break'> </span> things that happened that day<span class='line-break'> </span> and of the people that was<span class='line-break'> </span> liveing them that have passed a<span class='line-break'> </span> way.  Preacher Damron [?] staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> our <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a> the night before Otho was<span class='line-break'> </span> born.  He is <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.  Henry Henry<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield &amp; <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wooding</a> are<span class='line-break'> </span> both gone and all have to go soon.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> is here with us yet I am<span class='line-break'> </span> glad for her to be here anytime<span class='line-break'> </span> she will.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has bin busy all<span class='line-break'> </span> day and has a <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> in a long time<span class='line-break'> </span> until this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1435">
<h3><a name="page-1435">Saturday November  5, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> fixed <span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a> and with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a> help <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> some wood.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben &amp; family <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a>.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> home.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smiths</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a><span class='line-break'> </span> Smith carried me to White<span class='line-break'> </span> Falls.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> went with<span class='line-break'> </span> us.  I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> and caught several<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  We stopped at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> There was several men<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Hubbard</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and Little <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack</a> was there.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am always glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> any of the grand children.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8267' title='Martha Miller'>Martha Miller</a> (col) <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> for Marvin so that<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese could go with me<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  I know I am a bother<span class='line-break'> </span> some times but it wont last <span class='line-break'> </span> long.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1436">
<h3><a name="page-1436">Sunday November  6, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I went to <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Reynols</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and spent the day.  Posey &amp; Nancy K [?]<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  Mollie had a good<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I enjoyed my visit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I walked up there.  <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> brought<span class='line-break'> </span> me home on <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnsons</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia</a> &amp; Charlott all come<span class='line-break'> </span> with me home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/7651' title='Janie Brumfield'>Janie</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7649' title='Emmett Brumfield'>Emet Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> was here late this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; family went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/7991' title='train'>train</a> was<span class='line-break'> </span> late so it was dark when<span class='line-break'> </span> they got home.  Jim has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1437">
<h3><a name="page-1437">Monday November  7, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> to <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owens</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> got the stiches taken out of<span class='line-break'> </span> her lip. I do hope she will<span class='line-break'> </span> not have any more trouble<span class='line-break'> </span> of that sort. <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> went to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8218' title='Mr Kellie'>Mr Kellies</a> then they stripped<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>. They are at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helping <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie tobacco</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Woddings to see <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Woding</a>. She was not at<span class='line-break'> </span> home. <a href='../subjects/8071' title='Mrs Kent'>Mrs Kent</a> was and she<span class='line-break'> </span> had a good visit. <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp;<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> and I went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>. <a href='../subjects/8267' title='Martha Miller'>Martha Miller</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> from there this evening. I know<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie will miss her so much.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1438">
<h3><a name="page-1438">Tuesday November  8, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> served as<span class='line-break'> </span> one of the judges at the elect<span class='line-break'> </span> tion.  He sent <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a><span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> and voted.  We voted the<span class='line-break'> </span> Democrat ticket.  We went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> a while.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a>/Moses as was<span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  We had a pleasant<span class='line-break'> </span> visit.  Josie went to see<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has<span class='line-break'> </span> sore <a href='../subjects/167' title='hogs feet'>feet</a> so that they <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hardly walk.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1439">
<h3><a name="page-1439">Wednesday November  9, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7708' title='Mabel Brumfield'>Mabel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> has <a href='../subjects/8443' title='sore feet'>sore feet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  Found them<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8224' title='well'>well</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nothing happened today<span class='line-break'> </span> worth writing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We got the <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a><span class='line-break'> </span> news telling that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8199' title='Elbert Lee Trinkle'>Trinkle</a> is elected just<span class='line-break'> </span> as I expected.<span class='line-break'> </span> Hope he may make a <span class='line-break'> </span> good govonor.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1440">
<h3><a name="page-1440">Thursday November 10, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Jim &amp; Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco.  Josie helped to<span class='line-break'> </span> tye this evening.  I stayed at<span class='line-break'> </span> the house and mended some<span class='line-break'> </span> overalls.  Franklin &amp; Mabel<span class='line-break'> </span> went to the barn but did not<span class='line-break'> </span> stay long.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got dinner.  I ironed<span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got the light engine to<span class='line-break'> </span> start at twelve oclock.<span class='line-break'> </span> We was all glad that it<span class='line-break'> </span> started with out a trip to<span class='line-break'> </span> Gretna.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Edna went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.<span class='line-break'> </span> I have not seen any of<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins folks today.<span class='line-break'> </span> Oh how I am going to miss<span class='line-break'> </span> them when they are gone<span class='line-break'> </span> if I live to see that time.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben have not come from the barn yet.<span class='line-break'> </span> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1441">
<h3><a name="page-1441">Friday November 11, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben &amp; Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco all day and<span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  Josie and I got<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Josie ironed some<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins.  They<span class='line-break'> </span> were well.  Normon Booker<span class='line-break'> </span> brought two loads of<span class='line-break'> </span> stalk feed<span class='line-break'> </span> there this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am going to miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvins family so<span class='line-break'> </span> much. I dont like to<span class='line-break'> </span> think a bout there moveing.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1442">
<h3><a name="page-1442">Saturday November 12, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A colde windy day.  Ben<span class='line-break'> </span> stripped tobacco.  He finished a<span class='line-break'> </span> curing.  Henry tied all the time<span class='line-break'> </span> that Ben was sorting and Josie<span class='line-break'> </span> part of the time.  Jim went<span class='line-break'> </span> to Chatham.  Today was Nellies<span class='line-break'> </span> birth day.  Reese Smith carried<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and Paul and I went.<span class='line-break'> </span> I bought several things.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reubin and Robbert Reynols<span class='line-break'> </span> come with Reese as far as<span class='line-break'> </span> their home.  They had bin to<span class='line-break'> </span> Black Stone to play football<span class='line-break'> </span> and was on their way back<span class='line-break'> </span> to Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie ironed to day and got dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> and supper.  I went to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Carrie was ironing.<span class='line-break'> </span> Henry &amp; Ben went to Renan<span class='line-break'> </span> late this evening.  Ben bought <span class='line-break'> </span> a peice of beef for Sundays<span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1443">
<h3><a name="page-1443">Sunday November 13, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  There was ice<span class='line-break'> </span> a plenty this morning.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Kate Harveys this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Went by Reynols's and<span class='line-break'> </span> come back by there.  Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield come with Posie<span class='line-break'> </span> from Gretna.  Johnson brought<span class='line-break'> </span> us home.  Posie &amp; Charlott<span class='line-break'> </span> come with us.  I was glad to get<span class='line-break'> </span> to ride but hate to be a trouble.<span class='line-break'> </span> I eat dinner with Kate.<span class='line-break'> </span> Dr Wiggonton &amp; Pearl was<span class='line-break'> </span> there.  I was glad to see<span class='line-break'> </span> them.  Ben &amp; Josie staid at<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  I did not see Carrie<span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  The little boys was<span class='line-break'> </span> here a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that Jim got<span class='line-break'> </span> home and did not have to<span class='line-break'> </span> walk.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1444">
<h3><a name="page-1444">Monday November 14, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A rainy morning.  Henry went<span class='line-break'> </span> to school.  Edna staid at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim &amp; Ben helped Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> load on his tobacco &amp; he helped<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben load his.  They intend going<span class='line-break'> </span> to Gretna in the morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> Josie made Edna some pettie<span class='line-break'> </span> coats &amp; the baby some gowns.<span class='line-break'> </span> I got up at five this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> and got breakfast.  Had beef steak.<span class='line-break'> </span> I milked the cow &amp; fed all of <span class='line-break'> </span> the cows.  Fed the chickens.  Put <span class='line-break'> </span> on to boil some beef and potatoes<span class='line-break'> </span> and peas.  Toasted some coffee<span class='line-break'> </span> and churned.  Made bread and<span class='line-break'> </span> coffee and finished dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span> Kate Harvey come to Marvins<span class='line-break'> </span> and come here a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span> Reese was to take her home<span class='line-break'> </span> but he was so late getting<span class='line-break'> </span> home I guess she was gone.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1445">
<h3><a name="page-1445">Tuesday November 15, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A Beautiful day. We got up at three oclock and got breakfast for Ben. He started for Gretna Marvin went two. They got there OK but the tobacco solde for so near nothing they loaded it on and brought it home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim stripped on his all day. Josie got dinner. I sewed on my quilt in the morning in the evening I went to George Bliars. They were stripping tobacco at Blairs. Ren &amp; Ethel Worsham and Cordie Blair was gone to LynchBurg. Josie and the little children went to see Carrie a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben never got home until after nine oclock tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1446">
<h3><a name="page-1446">Blank</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1447">
<h3><a name="page-1447">Thursday November 17, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Warm for<span class='line-break'> </span> November  Jim worked on tobacco.<span class='line-break'> </span> John Hutcherson went to<span class='line-break'> </span> Danville.  He had tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> for Mr Kent &amp; Marvin<span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben.  I do hope it<span class='line-break'> </span> may sell so that they<span class='line-break'> </span> will be paid for carrieing<span class='line-break'> </span> it to Danville.<span class='line-break'> </span> Alcie Callant[?] washed<span class='line-break'> </span> for Josie today.  Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> Cordie Blair come<span class='line-break'> </span> to see us this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span> The chldren went to<span class='line-break'> </span> school.  Ben is in Danville<span class='line-break'> </span> to night if they had<span class='line-break'> </span> no bad luck.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-1448">
<h3><a name="page-1448">Friday November 18, 1921</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Very warm for Nov.<span class='line-break'> </span> Jim stripped tobacco all day<span class='line-break'> </span> and tonight.  Henry went to<span class='line-break'> </span> the barn tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went to Danville yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span> He has just come home <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  He solde tobacco<span class='line-break'> </span> today.  Solde very well for<span class='line-break'> </span> what it was.
